## The Ice Witch of Iceridge (Ylva Frostborn)
*Medium fey, neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 15 (18 with mage armor)
**Hit Points** :: 117 (18d8 + 36)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![The Ice Witch of Iceridge (Ylva Frostborn)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-the-ice-witch-ylva-frostborn.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 10 (+0) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 20 (+5) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Constitution +6, Charisma +9
**Skills** :: Arcana +6, Insight +7, Nature +6, Perception +7, Survival +7
**Damage Immunities** :: Cold
**Condition Immunities** :: Charmed
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 17
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Primordial
**Challenge** :: 11 (7,200 XP)
___
***Fey Step (Recharge 4-6).*** :: Bonus action to teleport 30 ft. Each creature within 5 ft. of starting position takes 3d10 cold damage (DC 17 Cha save for half).
***Fey Ancestry.*** :: Advantage vs. being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
***Spellcasting.*** :: 11th-level sorcerer. Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit.
***Sorcery Points.*** :: 11 points for Metamagic.
***- Twinned Spell.*** :: Target second creature with single-target spell
***- Empowered Spell.*** :: Reroll damage dice
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Frostbite, Mage Hand, Message, Ray of Frost
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Mage Armor*, Shield, Ice Knife
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Hold Person, Misty Step, Snilloc's Snowball Swarm
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Sleet Storm, Counterspell, Fly
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Ice Storm, Wall of Ice
***5th level (2 slots).*** :: Cone of Cold, Hold Monster
***6th level (1 slot).*** :: Investiture of Ice
***Cold Immunity.*** :: Immune to cold damage, never feels cold.
***Winter's Child.*** :: Can walk on ice and snow without leaving tracks or slipping.
***Animal Affinity.*** :: Advantage on Animal Handling with arctic animals. They're naturally friendly.
***Ancient Oath.*** :: Bound by ancient pact to protect Iceridge. Can't permanently leave region.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two frost touch attacks or casts two cantrips.
***Frost Touch.*** :: Melee Spell Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft. ***Hit.*** 4d10 cold damage, target's speed reduced by 10 ft. until end of next turn.::
***Cast a Spell.*** :: Casts a spell.
***Summon Winter Wolves (1/Day).*** :: Summons 2d4 winter wolves that serve for 1 hour.
### Reactions
***Shield.*** :: Cast Shield for +5 AC.
***Counterspell.*** :: Counter spell of 3rd level or lower.
***Frozen Defense.*** :: When hit by melee attack, attacker takes 2d10 cold damage.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Cantrip.** :: Casts a cantrip.
**Teleport (Costs 2).** :: Uses Fey Step if available or Misty Step.
**Frozen Aura (Costs 3).** :: 20 ft. radius around her becomes difficult terrain (ice) for 1 minute. Creatures starting turn there take 2d10 cold damage.
*"Winter is not cruel. It simply is. Humans mistake indifference for malice."*
}}

### Physical Description
Ethereally beautiful (5'10", 140 lbs) with pale, almost translucent skin. Long white hair flows like snow. Eyes are pale blue, shifting like winter sky. Wears flowing robes of ice-blue that seem woven from frost itself. Barefoot always, leaving no tracks. Surrounded by faint mist. White wolves follow her. Smells of pine and fresh snow. Voice sounds like wind through ice.
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}

\page
### Equipment
- **Robes:** Flowing ice-blue robes (never get dirty or wet)
- **Staff:** Ice Crystal Staff (acts as arcane focus)
- **Crown:** Circlet of ice crystals (permanent, part of her)
- **No armor needed:** Natural AC from fey nature
- **No shoes:** Walks barefoot in snow

### Personality
- Detached, observes humanity from outside
- Kind but alien in her kindness
- Protects community because of ancient oath
- Sees long-term (decades/centuries)
- Lonely but accepts isolation

**Secrets:**
1. **True Nature:** Winter eladrin bound by 200-year-old oath
2. **The Oath:** Protects something imprisoned beneath town
3. **Archfey Connection:** Serves an archfey of winter
4. **Limited Time:** Oath ends in 50 years - then she's free

**Plot Hooks:**
- Ice chamber awakening threatens her oath
- Needs party to help fulfill ancient duty
- Archfey summons her, leaving town vulnerable
- Miners transforming - she must intervene

---

### Background & History
Ylva was born during a blizzard that killed her mother and left her father's fingers blackened with frostbite. The village should have left her to die—winter's children rarely survived—but her father refused. She lived, and the cold followed her.

By ten, she could freeze water with a touch. By twenty, she could summon blizzards. The villagers drove her out, calling her cursed. She found refuge in the ice caves of Mount Frostpeak, where she's lived for sixty years, growing stronger and stranger.

She's not evil—she protects the mountain communities from avalanches and warns of deadly storms. But she's no longer entirely human. The ice has seeped into her soul, making her cold, patient, and difficult to understand. Those who approach her properly receive help; those who don't face the fury of winter.

### Connections
- **Friend:** The Frost Seer Eirlys (kindred spirits)
- **Rival:** Witch Mother Helga (old disagreement over a stolen bargain)
- **Protectorate:** Mountain villages that honor her
- **Enemy:** The fire cult that tried to kill her
- **Master:** The mountain itself (or something within it)

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Mountain's Voice:** Something speaks to her from within the mountain. She serves it without understanding what it is.
2. **The Fire Cult:** A cult of fire worshippers tried to kill her twenty years ago. She destroyed most of them but some survived.
3. **The Transformation:** She's becoming less human each year. Eventually she'll be pure ice, unable to interact with mortals.
4. **The Helga Bargain:** Stole a deal from Witch Mother Helga. The two have been enemies since.
5. **The Frozen Love:** Once loved a human. Froze him to preserve him when he was dying. He's still in the ice, preserved.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Mountain's Will:** The voice wants something. She needs help interpreting its desires.
2. **The Fire Cult Return:** The survivors are gathering strength. She needs allies against them.
3. **The Transformation Cure:** Seeking a way to slow or stop her transformation. Willing to reward help.
4. **The Helga Conflict:** The feud with Helga is escalating. Could use allies—or mediators.
5. **The Frozen Love:** Has found a way to thaw her lover safely. Needs help with the ritual.

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}

\page

## Forge-Master Thordak Lavaheart
*Medium humanoid (genasi), lawful neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (chain mail)
**Hit Points** :: 136 (16d8 + 64)
**Speed** :: 25 ft.

|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 20 (+5) | 12 (+1) | 18 (+4) | 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) | 12 (+1) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +9, Constitution +8, Intelligence +8
**Skills** :: Athletics +9, History +8, Insight +6, Perception +6, Smith's Tools +12 (expertise)
**Damage Resistances** :: Fire
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 16
**Languages** :: Common, Dwarvish, Ignan, Primordial

***Fire Resistance.*** :: Resistant to fire damage.
***Reach to the Blaze.*** :: Can cast Burning Hands (3rd level) 1/day.
***Darkvision.*** :: 60 ft.
***Master Smith.*** :: Advantage on all checks to craft, repair, or identify metal items. Can create items of up to very rare quality.
***Lava Heart.*** :: Survived falling in lava as child. Immune to extreme heat. Can touch molten metal safely.
***Legendary Craftsman.*** :: Can craft magical weapons and armor. Creates items in half normal time.

***Smith's Defense.*** :: When hit by metal weapon, can superheat it. Attacker takes 3d6 fire damage and must drop weapon (DC 16 Con save negates drop).
*"Iron bends. Steel breaks. But a proper dwarven weapon? That endures forever."*
}}

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Chain Mail (heat-resistant)
- **Primary:** Volcanic Warhammer +2 (legendary, family heirloom)
- **Tools:** Masterwork smith's tools (+2 to all checks)
- **Apron:** Red Dragon Hide Apron (fire immunity while worn)
- **Goggles:** Volcanic Goggles (can see through smoke/steam)

**Secret:** Unknowingly forged cursed weapon for Unbound agent!

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}

\page

### Background & History
Thordak's forge sits at the edge of an active volcanic vent, where he works metal in heat that would kill ordinary smiths. He's a dragonborn of red dragon heritage, immune to fire and capable of producing work that requires temperatures no normal forge can reach.

He learned his craft from a fire giant smith who owed his father a life debt. For twenty years, he trained in the volcanic depths, learning techniques unknown to surface races. When he emerged, he established a forge that produces the most heat-resistant equipment in the world.

The Ashwardens are his primary clients, but anyone willing to pay his prices and brave the journey receives his work. He's gruff, rude, and completely uninterested in social niceties. He cares only for craft and considers conversation a waste of smithing time.

### Connections
- **Client:** Grand Warden Volcanus Rex (primary contract)
- **Teacher:** Fire giant smith Ignak (still corresponds)
- **Rival:** Forge-Master Rurik Ironanvil (respects but competitive)
- **Apprentice:** One fire genasi who can survive the heat
- **Contact:** Something in the volcano (trades service for rare metals)

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Volcanic Entity:** Trades with something living in the magma. It provides metals that shouldn't exist.
2. **The Dragon Legacy:** His red dragon ancestor is still alive somewhere. He's received one message in his life.
3. **The Perfect Work:** Has spent decades on a masterwork for himself. Nearly complete.
4. **The Giant Debt:** His teacher's debt was paid, but Thordak owes the giant something now.
5. **The Volcanic Instability:** Knows the volcano is building toward an eruption. Hasn't told anyone.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Commission:** Offers to make something extraordinary if the party retrieves volcanic materials.
2. **The Giant Contact:** Needs a message delivered to his teacher in the deep volcanic reaches.
3. **The Volcanic Warning:** Shares his knowledge of the coming eruption if properly approached.
4. **The Entity Trade:** The volcanic entity wants something. Needs intermediaries.
5. **The Dragon Message:** Has received another message from his ancestor. Needs help responding.

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}

{{monster,frame,wide
## Sage Elminster Runereader
*Medium humanoid (human), neutral good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 12 (15 with mage armor)
**Hit Points** :: 71 (13d8 + 13)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Sage Elminster Runereader](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-sage-elminster-runereader.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 8 (-1) | 12 (+1) | 12 (+1) | 20 (+5) | 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +9, Wisdom +8
**Skills** :: Arcana +13 (expertise), History +13 (expertise), Investigation +9, Perception +8, Religion +9
**Senses** :: Passive Perception 18
**Languages** :: Common, Dwarvish, Draconic, Elvish, Giant, Ancient Common
**Challenge** :: 9 (5,000 XP)
___
***Spellcasting.*** :: 9th-level wizard. DC 17, +9 to hit.
***Cantrips.*** :: Light, Mage Hand, Message, Prestidigitation
***1st (4).*** :: Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
***2nd (3).*** :: Arcane Lock, Knock, See Invisibility
***3rd (3).*** :: Dispel Magic, Glyph of Warding, Tongues
***4th (3).*** :: Arcane Eye, Stone Shape
***5th (1).*** :: Legend Lore, Passwall
***Rune Expert.*** :: Can read and understand any runic script. Advantage on checks to identify magical symbols.
***Ancient Knowledge.*** :: Has studied pre-Worldrend sites for 50 years. Knows their construction, purpose, dangers.
***Glyph Specialist.*** :: Can identify and safely disarm magical glyphs and wards.
### Actions
***Quarterstaff.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +2 to hit. ***Hit.*** 1d6-1 bludgeoning.::
***Cast a Spell.*** :: Casts prepared spell.
***Runic Analysis (Special).*** :: Spends 10 minutes studying runes to determine their function, age, and activation conditions.
### Reactions
***Counterspell.*** :: Counter spell of 3rd level or lower.
***Runic Warning.*** :: When ally about to trigger magical trap, can shout warning (ally gains advantage on save, reaction).
*"These runes predate the Worldrend. They're not decoration - they're warnings."*
}}

### Equipment
- **Robes:** Scholar's robes
- **Staff:** Walking staff (mundane)
- **Spectacles:** Reading glasses (advantage on deciphering text)
- **Books:** 12 notebooks full of runic research
- **Tools:** Runic transcription kit

### Background & History
Elminster's name is a deliberate joke—his parents were adventurers who thought naming their son after a famous wizard would bring him luck. It worked; he's become one of the foremost scholars of runic magic in Thaldros, able to read inscriptions that have baffled others for centuries.

His specialty is pre-Worldrend text, the ancient scripts that were used before the world was torn apart. He's spent sixty years collecting rubbings, copying inscriptions, and developing translation methods. His crowning achievement is a partial dictionary of the Elder Script, the language used by the civilization that caused the Worldrend.

He works from a cluttered study in the Silverpine Academy, surrounded by books, scrolls, and strange artifacts. He's absent-minded about everyday matters but razor-sharp about his field. Students simultaneously adore and fear him—he's brilliant but demands excellence.

### Connections
- **Institution:** Silverpine Academy (senior professor)
- **Student:** Six doctoral candidates in ancient languages
- **Collaborator:** Professor Elara Moonwhisper (combines astronomy with his linguistics)
- **Correspondent:** Scholars across both continents
- **Enemy:** Treasure hunters who destroy inscriptions while looting

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Complete Translation:** Has secretly translated more Elder Script than he's published. Some texts are too dangerous.
2. **The Worldrend Cause:** His translations suggest the Worldrend was deliberate—someone meant to tear the world apart.
3. **The Warning:** One text appears to describe how to prevent a second Worldrend. He's still deciphering it.
4. **The Stolen Artifact:** Stole a key artifact from treasure hunters who would have destroyed it. Technically illegal.
5. **The Immortality Hints:** Some texts describe techniques for extending life. He's tempted to try them.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Translation Project:** Has a text that resists translation. Needs adventurers to investigate its source.
2. **The Dangerous Knowledge:** Ready to share what he knows about the Worldrend—but only with those he trusts.
3. **The Artifact Problem:** The stolen artifact is being sought. Needs help either hiding it or legitimizing his possession.
4. **The Field Expedition:** Needs to visit a ruin to study inscriptions in context. Needs protection.
5. **The Prevention Theory:** Believes he's found instructions to prevent catastrophe. Needs help implementing them.

## Engineer Mira Steamvent
*Small humanoid (rock gnome), neutral good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (reinforced work jacket, Dex)
**Hit Points** :: 82 (15d6 + 30)
**Speed** :: 25 ft.
![Engineer Mira Steamvent](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-engineer-mira-steamvent.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}

|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 8 (-1) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 20 (+5) | 14 (+2) | 10 (+0) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +8, Wisdom +5, Constitution +5
**Skills** :: Arcana +8, History +8, Investigation +11, Perception +5,
**Damage Resistances** :: Fire (heat-resistant gear)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 15
**Languages** :: Common, Gnomish, Dwarvish, Primordial (fire)
**Challenge** :: 7 (2,900 XP)
___
***Gnome Cunning.*** :: Advantage on Int, Wis, and Cha saves against magic.
***Artificer's Lore.*** :: Add double proficiency to History checks on magic items
***Engineering Genius.*** :: Can analyze any mechanical system in 1 minute.
***Heat Adapted.*** :: Immune to extreme heat environmental effects.
***Improvised Solutions.*** :: Can jury-rig temporary repairs. As an action,
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two wrench attacks or two crossbow attacks.
***Heavy Wrench.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d8+3 bludgeoning damage. On a critical hit, target's armor or::
shield AC is reduced by 1 until repaired.
***Light Crossbow.*** :: Ranged Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, range 80/320 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d8+3 piercing damage.::
***Steam Vent (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Releases superheated steam in 15-foot cone.
DC 16 Dex save. 6d6 fire damage, half on success. Creatures that fail
are blinded until end of their next turn.
***Emergency Shutoff (1/Day).*** :: Can immediately stop any mechanical system
within 60 feet that she can see, including constructs. Constructs make
DC 16 Con save or are stunned for 1 round.
### Reactions
***Danger Sense.*** :: When Mira or a creature within 30 feet triggers a trap
or mechanical hazard, she can shout a warning. Target gains +5 to
their saving throw.
*"Lava doesn't negotiate. Neither do I. The systems work or people die."*
}}

### Background & History
Mira was born with a gift for understanding machines that borders on magical—she can hear when gears are misaligned, feel when pressure is building dangerously, sense the flow of steam and water through pipes. She's used this talent to become the Ashwardens' primary engineer, designing systems that contain volcanic forces.

Her containment domes, pressure release valves, and early warning networks have saved tens of thousands of lives. She works constantly, driven by the memory of her hometown's destruction by volcanic eruption when she was twelve. She survived; three thousand others didn't.

She splits her time between the Ashgate engineering works and field installations across volcanic regions. She's practical, blunt, and impatient with those who don't share her urgency. Every day without proper containment is a day someone might die, and she can't afford to waste time on politics or niceties.
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page
### Connections
- **Superior:** Warden Commander Ignis Ashborn (close working relationship)
- **Supplier:** Forge-Master Thordak Lavaheart (provides specialized components)
- **Team:** Twenty engineers and fifty technicians
- **Rival:** Artificer Tobias Gearwise (different engineering philosophy)
- **Ghost:** The three thousand dead (drives her forward)

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Impossible Project:** Designing a system to redirect a super-eruption. Theoretically possible; practically untested.
2. **The Survivor's Guilt:** Blames herself for not warning her hometown in time, even though she was twelve.
3. **The Magical Component:** Her "intuition" might actually be a magical gift. She's refused to investigate.
4. **The Ashgate Weakness:** Knows Ashgate's containment system has a critical flaw she can't fix with current resources.
5. **The Alternative Plan:** Has designed evacuation systems for when containment fails. Hopes never to use them.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Field Installation:** Needs protection while installing containment systems in dangerous territory.
2. **The Resource Crisis:** The Ashgate flaw requires materials she can't obtain through normal channels.
3. **The Super-Eruption Test:** Wants to test her redirection system on a minor volcanic event. Needs observers.
4. **The Magic Question:** Finally ready to investigate whether her gift is magical. Needs discrete help.
5. **The Emergency Protocol:** A major eruption is imminent. Needs all hands helping with evacuation.


**Key Details:**
- Manages complex system of channels, vents, and cooling chambers
- Keeps town from being consumed by volcanic activity
- Brilliant but exhausted - works 18-hour days
- Covered in soot, goggles, carries blueprint tubes everywhere
- Invented three new cooling techniques
- Missing two fingers from early career accident
- Drinks coffee like water, rarely sleeps

**Personality:**
- Direct, no-nonsense, impatient with incompetence
- Brilliant under pressure
- Deeply responsible for town's safety
- Sarcastic dark humor about death by lava
- Softens around genuine technical curiosity
- Secretly terrified system will fail

**Secrets:**
1. **System Failing:** Recent tremors damaged core systems - holding together with patches
2. **Ancient Infrastructure:** Current systems built on pre-Worldrend dwarven engineering
3. **The Deep Crack:** New fissure opening beneath town, she's hiding severity
4. **Sabotage:** Someone tampering with valves - causing "accidents"
5. **The Emergency Plan:** Has evacuation protocol, but it only saves half the town
6. **Unbound Interest:** They approached her for information about deep tunnels

**Plot Hooks:**
- System catastrophically failing - needs emergency repair team
- Her assistant murdered - saboteur still active
- Ancient mechanisms activating, she can't understand them
- Needs party to reach deep valve chamber through hostile tunnels
- The Deep Crack connects to something that shouldn't be disturbed
- She's kidnapped - no one else can prevent disaster

**Connections:**
- Works closely with Forge-Master Thordak
- Reports concerns to Quarry-Master Borin (he dismisses them)
- Studied at Silverpine University under Professor Miranda Questseeker
- Corresponds with Merchant League about funding (denied)
- Has sent warning letters to King Aldric (no response)

**Engineering Knowledge:**
- Expert in geology, physics, structural engineering
- Can calculate pressure, flow rates, structural integrity instantly
- Designs contingency systems and fail-safes
- Improvises solutions with available materials
- Understands ancient dwarven technical documentation

**Equipment:**
- Masterwork tools (advantage on all checks)
- *Goggles of darkvision* and heat vision
- *Ring of fire resistance*
- Emergency cooling grenades (homebrew items)
- Portable pressure gauge (magical sensor)

## Quarry-Master Borin Stonecutter
*Medium humanoid (shield dwarf), lawful neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 18 (half plate, shield)
**Hit Points** :: 112 (15d8 + 45)
**Speed** :: 25 ft.
![Quarry-Master Borin Stonecutter](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-quarry-master-borin-stonecutter.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 18 (+4) | 12 (+1) | 16 (+3) | 12 (+1) | 14 (+2) | 10 (+0) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +7, Constitution +6
**Skills** :: Athletics +10, History +4, Intimidation +3, Perception +5,
**Damage Resistances** :: Poison
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 15
**Languages** :: Common, Dwarvish, Terran (basic)
**Challenge** :: 8 (3,900 XP)
___
***Dwarven Resilience.*** :: Advantage on saves against poison.
***Stonecunning.*** :: Double proficiency on History checks related to stonework.
***Quarry Veteran.*** :: 60 years of experience. Advantage on checks to identify
***Indomitable (2/Day).*** :: Can reroll a failed saving throw.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes three attacks with his warhammer or two thrown hammers.
***Stonecutter's Hammer (Family Heirloom).*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit,::
***reach 5 ft., one target. Hit.*** :: 2d8+5 bludgeoning damage. Against constructs
and objects, deals an extra 1d8 damage. This ancient dwarven hammer
glows faintly near active golem runes.
***Throwing Hammer.*** :: Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, range 20/60 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d6+4 bludgeoning damage.::
***Leadership (Recharges after Short Rest).*** :: For 1 minute, Borin can issue
a special command as a bonus action. Any ally within 30 feet who can
hear him adds 1d4 to their attack rolls and saving throws.
***Stone Sense (1/Day).*** :: Borin places his hand on stone and concentrates
for 1 minute. He learns the location of all creatures and hollow spaces
within 120 feet that are touching the same stone surface.
### Reactions
***Parry.*** :: Adds +3 to AC against one melee attack that would hit him.
Must be wielding his hammer.
***Protect the Workers.*** :: When an ally within 5 feet is hit by an attack,
Borin can use his reaction to become the target instead.
*"Stone's been dead for millennia. If it's moving now, that's a problem."*
}}

### Background & History
The Stonecutter clan has managed the great stone quarries south of the Ironspines for eight generations. Borin inherited the operation at fifty when his mother retired, and has spent the last century turning a profitable business into an essential one.

His stone builds the castles, bridges, and monuments of a dozen kingdoms. He employs three thousand workers across multiple quarries and has developed techniques that produce stone of unprecedented quality. His personal fortune rivals some noble houses, but he lives simply—wealth is for reinvestment, not display.

He's a patient negotiator, willing to wait years for the right deal. He's also utterly ruthless when crossed; anyone who cheats him discovers their stone shipments delayed indefinitely, their competitors suddenly well-supplied. He doesn't need to threaten—his control of the market speaks for itself.

### Connections
- **Employees:** Three thousand quarry workers
- **Ally:** Master Miner Grimnir Deepdelve (complementary businesses)
- **Client:** Every major construction project in Thaldros
- **Rival:** Lesser quarry operators he's slowly absorbing
- **Contact:** Something ancient in the deepest quarry

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Ancient Quarry:** The deepest quarry cuts into pre-Worldrend ruins. He's been quietly excavating.
2. **The Living Stone:** Has discovered stone that seems to respond to commands. Hasn't told anyone.
3. **The Worker Treatment:** His workers are well-paid because they've seen things they could reveal.
4. **The Noble Leverage:** Has dirt on multiple noble houses from construction projects. Emergency insurance.
5. **The Succession Problem:** No children, no clear heir. Worries about his legacy.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Deep Discovery:** Found something in the pre-Worldrend ruins. Needs experts to assess it.
2. **The Living Stone:** Wants to understand the responsive stone. Needs magical investigation.
3. **The Heir Search:** Looking for someone worthy to inherit. Tests likely candidates.
4. **The Competition Problem:** Someone is trying to break his market control. Needs the source identified.
5. **The Simple Job:** Just needs reliable protection for a valuable shipment. Honest work.


**Key Details:**
- Manages Stonehaven quarries for 60 years
- Recent awakening of stone golems baffles him
- Stocky, powerful, grey beard to his belt
- Hands like granite from decades of stone work
- Carries ancient stonecutter's hammer (family heirloom)
- Deeply troubled by golem situation
- Former military engineer, knows fortifications

**Personality:**
- Pragmatic, straightforward, salt-of-earth
- Proud of his work and his quarry
- Protective of his workers (23 under his command)
- Dismissive of "magic nonsense" (despite evidence)
- Stubborn about admitting he needs help
- Deeply disturbed that stone is "waking up"

**Secrets:**
1. **Quarry Location:** Built on pre-Worldrend golem factory
2. **Active Runes:** His quarrying disturbed ancient activation runes
3. **Lost Workers:** Three workers killed by golems, he's covering it up
4. **The Master Rune:** Found central control rune, afraid to touch it
5. **Guilt:** Ignored warnings from Sage Elminster about quarry location
6. **Corporation Pressure:** Merchant League demanding he keep operating despite danger

**Plot Hooks:**
- Golems attacking workers - needs immediate help
- Party hired to investigate golem origins
- Central control rune could shut them down or awaken them all
- Workers trapped in quarry by golem patrol
- Golem army could march on town if fully activated
- Ancient defense protocols recognizing modern people as intruders

**Connections:**
- Trained Master Miner Grimnir decades ago
- Cousin of Thane Durgan Ironforge (historical house founder)
- Reports to Merchant League officials (who pressure him)
- Dismisses Sage Elminster's warnings (huge mistake)
- Knows Forge-Master Thordak from military engineering days

**Combat Notes:**
- Veteran fighter (CR 8)
- Warhammer: +10 to hit, 2d8+6 bludgeoning
- Stone Sense: Advantage on checks related to stone and earth
- Quarry Master: Can judge structural stability instantly
- Defensive stance: +4 AC against constructs

{{monster,frame,wide
## Elder Thalindra Oakheart
*Medium humanoid (elf), neutral good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (barkskin armor, natural)
**Hit Points** :: 142 (19d8 + 57)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Elder Thalindra Oakheart](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-elder-thalindra-oakheart.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 10 (+0) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 18 (+4) | 22 (+6) | 16 (+3) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +9, Wisdom +11, Charisma +8
**Skills** :: Arcana +9, History +14 (expertise), Insight +11, Medicine +11, Nature +14 (expertise), Perception +11, Religion +9, Survival +11
**Damage Resistances** :: Poison; Bludgeoning, Piercing from nonmagical attacks
**Condition Immunities** :: Charmed, Frightened (while within 100 ft. of Heart Oak)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 21, Tremorsense 30 ft. (through tree roots)
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Druidic, Ancient Elvish, Primordial, Celestial
**Challenge** :: 13 (10,000 XP)
___
***Fey Ancestry.*** :: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
***Trance.*** :: Meditates 4 hours instead of sleeping.
***Ancient Memory.*** :: Can perfectly recall any event she's witnessed in her long life.
***Spellcasting.*** :: 15th-level druid (Circle of the Land - Forest). Spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks.
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Druidcraft, Guidance, Mending, Shillelagh, Thorn Whip
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Cure Wounds, Detect Magic, Entangle, Goodberry, Speak with Animals
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Barkskin*, Lesser Restoration, Pass without Trace, Spike Growth
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Call Lightning, Dispel Magic, Plant Growth, Speak with Plants
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Blight, Dominate Beast, Freedom of Movement, Grasping Vine
***5th level (2 slots).*** :: Commune with Nature, Greater Restoration, Tree Stride
***6th level (1 slot).*** :: Heal, Transport via Plants, Wall of Thorns
***7th level (1 slot).*** :: Regenerate
***8th level (1 slot).*** :: Animal Shapes
***Heart Oak Bond.*** :: While within 1 mile of the Heart Oak, Thalindra:
***Ancient Wisdom.*** :: Has lived through the Worldrend and Age of Strife. Can provide historical context for any event in the last 800 years. Advantage on all Intelligence checks related to history or lore.
***Tree Stride (At Will).*** :: Can use *tree stride* without expending a spell slot when within forest terrain, traveling between trees within 500 ft. (ritual takes 1 minute).
***Nature's Sanctuary.*** :: Animals and plant creatures must succeed on DC 19 Wisdom save to attack her. On success, immune for 24 hours.
***Timeless Body.*** :: Does not age magically. Appears middle-aged despite her centuries.
***Blessing of the Heart Oak (1/Day).*** :: Can channel the Heart Oak's power to cast any healing spell she knows without expending a spell slot, at 9th level.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with Oakheart Staff, or casts a cantrip and uses staff once.
***Oakheart Staff (Shillelagh Enhanced).*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +11 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d8+6 magical bludgeoning damage plus 2d6 radiant damage (tree's blessing).::
***Special.*** :: This ancient staff was carved from a branch of the Heart Oak 600 years ago. On critical hit, target must succeed DC 19 Wisdom save or be stunned until end of Thalindra's next turn.
***Thorn Whip.*** :: Ranged Spell Attack: +11 to hit, range 30 ft., one creature. ***Hit.*** 3d6 piercing damage, and target is pulled 10 ft. toward Thalindra if Large or smaller.::
***Entangling Roots (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Thalindra causes roots to burst from the ground in a 20-foot radius centered on her. Each creature in the area must succeed on a DC 19 Strength save or be restrained by roots (escape DC 19). The roots last 1 minute and have AC 15, 50 HP.
***Call the Ancient Forest (1/Day).*** :: Thalindra summons the forest's aid. For 1 minute:
- All plant growth in a 100-foot radius becomes difficult terrain for enemies
- She can cast *speak with plants* at will
- Allied druids and rangers within range gain advantage on attack rolls
- She gains +2 to spell save DC (becomes DC 21)
### Reactions
***Nature's Ward.*** :: When a creature within 30 ft. is hit by an attack, Thalindra causes vines to deflect the blow, granting +5 AC against that attack (potentially causing it to miss).
***Treespeech Warning.*** :: When danger approaches the Heart Oak, she is instantly aware and can use *tree stride* as a reaction to teleport to its location.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Cantrip.** :: Casts a druid cantrip.
**Move.** :: Uses tree stride to teleport to any tree within 60 ft.
**Healing Touch (Costs 2).** :: Touches a creature and restores 3d8+6 hit points.
**Command Forest (Costs 2).** :: Commands plants in a 30-foot radius to restrain one creature (DC 19 Strength save).
*"The Heart Oak has stood for three thousand years. It shall stand three thousand more, or I shall fall with it."*
}}
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Physical Description
Ancient and ethereal (5'10", 130 lbs) with a presence that commands respect without words. Skin has a faint golden-brown hue like aged oak, with subtle patterns resembling wood grain visible in certain lights. Silver-white hair flows past her waist, often adorned with living vines, flowers, and autumn leaves that grow naturally from it. Eyes are deep forest green with golden flecks, seeming to hold the wisdom of centuries. Moves with slow, deliberate grace. Wears flowing robes of deep green embroidered with golden leaves. The Oakheart Staff is always at her side, pulsing with faint green light. Her hands are gnarled like ancient wood but gentle. Small roots occasionally sprout from her footsteps when she stands still too long.

### Equipment
- **Staff:** Oakheart Staff (legendary, carved from Heart Oak, never broken, +2 quarterstaff, functions as Staff of the Woodlands)
- **Armor:** Living Bark Armor (AC 16, made from shed bark of Heart Oak, regrows when damaged, grants resistance to poison)
- **Robes:** Ancient Elvish ceremonial robes (deep green with gold leaf patterns)
- **Crown:** Circlet of Autumn Leaves (continuously sheds and regrows golden leaves, grants advantage on Charisma checks with fey)
- **Amulet:** Acorn of the First Tree (contains seed from pre-Worldrend era, grants *speak with plants* at will)
- **Ring:** Ring of Regeneration (1 HP per 10 minutes)
- **Belt:** Belt of Living Wood (contains emergency healing potions stored in wood-grain pockets)
- **Pouch:** Component pouch with rare herbs and crystals
- **Book:** Personal journal spanning 847 years (invaluable historical record)
- **Potions:** 2 potions of supreme healing, 1 potion of vitality, 3 potions of greater healing
- **Seeds:** Rare magical plant seeds (moonflower, starlight rose, dreamvine)

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks slowly, choosing each word with centuries of consideration
- Often pauses mid-sentence to listen to the forest
- Touches trees when passing, as if greeting old friends
- Refers to events from centuries ago as if they were yesterday
- Has a serene smile that carries profound sadness
- Never raises her voice, yet commands absolute attention
- Smells of oak leaves, morning dew, and ancient forest

**Ideals:**
- **Life:** "All living things are connected. To harm the forest is to harm ourselves."
- **Memory:** "I am the keeper of memories that would otherwise be lost to time."
- **Balance:** "The forest takes and gives in equal measure. So must we."
- **Hope:** "I have seen empires fall and forests regrow. There is always hope."

**Bonds:**
- The Heart Oak (would die to protect it)
- Her apprentice, Elder Silverbark (403 years old, still young in her eyes)
- The people of Oakenheart (both human and elf)
- Ancient oaths made during the Age of Strife
- The memory of her beloved, lost in the Worldrend
- The forest itself, which she considers her body's extension

**Flaws:**
- Impossibly patient to the point of inaction (centuries have taught her patience, sometimes too much)
- Guilt over surviving the Worldrend when so many died
- Secretly fears the Heart Oak's death means her death
- Sometimes loses track of "modern" concerns (what happened 50 years ago is "recent" to her)
- Struggles to understand human urgency and short-term thinking
- The Heart Oak's illness is draining her own life force (she hides this)
- Knows she's dying with the tree but refuses to leave it

### Background & History
Thalindra has led the village of Oakheart Grove for three centuries, watching generations of humans come and go while the elven core of the community remains. She's seen wars, plagues, and natural disasters; she's guided her people through all of them.

She was a druid of considerable power in her youth, but chose to focus on community leadership rather than mystical pursuits. She still maintains a connection to the great oak at the village center, which was planted by her grandmother and will likely outlive her grandchildren.

Her leadership style is gentle guidance rather than command. She rarely orders anything directly, instead asking questions that lead people to the right conclusions. Some find this maddening; others appreciate being treated as capable adults. She's been doing it so long she's forgotten any other approach.
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Connections
- **Community:** Oakheart Grove (800 residents)
- **Advisors:** Circle of village elders (five others)
- **Druid Contact:** Archdruid Silvaris Oakenheart (old friend)
- **Trade Partner:** Various merchant caravans
- **Concern:** The young, restless elves leaving for cities

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Village Anchor:** She is mystically bound to Oakheart Grove. If she leaves, she dies within days.
2. **The Old War:** In her youth, she killed a human noble who was enslaving elves. Never told anyone.
3. **The Exodus Fear:** Young elves are leaving faster than they're replaced. The village may die within a century.
4. **The Sacred Trust:** Guards a portal to the Feywild that opens once per century. Next opening is soon.
5. **The Weary Heart:** Has been ready to die for decades. Stays alive only because she's needed.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Portal Preparation:** The Feywild portal opens soon. Needs help preparing for whatever comes through.
2. **The Youth Appeal:** Looking for ways to make the village attractive to young elves. Open to suggestions.
3. **The Old Crime:** Someone has discovered evidence of the killing. Needs help managing the situation.
4. **The Binding Investigation:** Wants to understand her bond to the village. Possibly break it.
5. **The Succession Planning:** Looking for someone to lead after her. Might see potential in party members.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Speaks in measured, poetic phrases
- Often quotes ancient proverbs in Elvish
- Touches the bark of the Heart Oak for comfort
- Makes tea from leaves and herbs during conversations
- Calls younger elves (under 300) "saplings"
- Refers to humans affectionately as "quick-bright flames"
- When stressed, leaves grow from her hair
- Her staff glows brighter when the Heart Oak is threatened

**Speech Pattern Examples:**
- "I have seen six hundred springs. Each taught me patience. This, too, shall pass."
- "When the Worldrend came, the trees wept. I hear their echoes still."
- "You ask what we should do? Child, I have watched mountains erode. I know what we *must* do."
- "The Heart Oak remembers the first words spoken in this land. It shares memories with me."

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}

\page

{{monster,frame,wide
## Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise
*Medium humanoid (human), lawful good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 15 (leather armor + shield)
**Hit Points** :: 68 (8d10 + 24)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-master-carpenter-aldric-woodwise.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 15 (+2) | 12 (+1) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +6, Constitution +6
**Skills** :: Athletics +6, Insight +5, Nature +5, Perception +5, Survival +5, Carpenter's Tools +8 (expertise), Woodcarver's Tools +8 (expertise)
**Senses** :: Passive Perception 15
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish (trade dialect)
**Challenge** :: 5 (1,800 XP)
___
***Master Craftsman.*** :: Has advantage on all checks using carpenter's tools or woodcarver's tools. Can identify the quality, age, and origin of any wooden object by touch.
***Wood Sense.*** :: Can detect the presence of wooden structures, hidden passages, or structural weaknesses in wooden buildings within 30 ft. Automatically notices concealed doors, trap doors, or architectural flaws.
***Expert Builder.*** :: Given appropriate tools and materials, can construct a basic wooden structure (house, bridge, wall) in half the normal time with superior quality (+2 AC for fortifications, +50% HP for structures).
***Sustainable Harvest.*** :: Knows exactly which trees can be safely harvested without damaging the forest. Has advantage on Nature checks related to forestry and tree health.
***Architect's Eye.*** :: Can assess building structural integrity at a glance. Knows if a building is dangerous, how much weight it can support, and where weak points are.
***Combat Carpenter.*** :: Years of chopping wood and construction have made him surprisingly effective in combat. His axe strikes are precise and devastating.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with Heirloom Greataxe or Handaxe.
***Heirloom Greataxe.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d12+3 slashing damage (two-handed) or 1d10+3 (versatile).::
***Special.*** :: This masterwork axe has been in his family for three generations. On critical hit, deals extra 2d12 damage.
***Handaxe +1.*** :: Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 20/60 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d6+4 slashing damage.::
***Hammer.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d6+3 bludgeoning damage.::
***Precise Strike (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Aldric makes a perfectly aimed strike with his axe, targeting a weak point. +5 to hit, and on hit deals 3d12+3 damage. If target is wearing wooden armor or is a plant creature, deals 4d12+3 instead.
***Improvised Defense (3/Day).*** :: Uses carpentry knowledge to quickly construct basic cover. As an action, creates a wooden barrier (AC 15, 30 HP) that provides half cover for up to 4 creatures.
### Reactions
***Defensive Chop.*** :: When a creature enters his reach, he can make an opportunity attack even if they used Disengage. +6 to hit, 1d10+3 damage.
***Structural Expertise.*** :: When an ally within 10 ft. is hit by an attack, Aldric can shout a warning about structural weaknesses. The ally gains +2 AC against that attack (potentially causing it to miss).
*"Every tree has a purpose. My job is to help it find that purpose—whether a beam, a bow, or a legacy."*
}}

### Physical Description
Solidly built (5'11", 210 lbs) with the powerful frame of someone who works with timber daily. Calloused hands covered in tiny scars and splinters. Short brown hair showing gray, usually dusted with sawdust. Brown eyes that constantly assess structures and quality. Full beard kept neat but practical. Wears leather work clothes reinforced at stress points. Smells of fresh-cut wood, pine sap, and linseed oil. Moves with the careful confidence of someone used to dangerous work. Always has wood shavings in his hair and on his clothes.
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Reinforced Leather (+1 leather armor, AC 12)
- **Shield:** Wooden Shield (masterwork, AC +2, can block one critical hit per day)
- **Primary Weapon:** Heirloom Greataxe (grandfather's axe, perfectly balanced, masterwork)
- **Secondary:** Handaxe +1 (masterwork throwing axe)
- **Tools:** Master carpenter's tools (worth 500 gp, include folding saw, precision chisels, measuring devices)
- **Belt:** Carpenter's Belt (contains hammer, nails, small tools, always within reach)
- **Boots:** Steel-toed Work Boots (protect feet, grant +2 to avoid being knocked prone)
- **Gloves:** Leather Work Gloves (prevent splinters, grant advantage on grip checks)
- **Backpack Contents:** Rope (100 ft.), block and tackle, wood samples, blueprints
- **Other:** Level, square, chalk line, plumb bob

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks in measured, thoughtful sentences
- Constantly fidgets with small wood pieces, carving as he talks
- Taps wooden structures to assess quality
- Quotes old carpentry sayings
- Protective of apprentices and trees
- Patient teacher but demanding master
- Takes pride in every piece he creates

**Ideals:**
- **Craftsmanship:** "If it's worth building, it's worth building right. No shortcuts."
- **Sustainability:** "Take only what the forest can spare. It'll provide forever."
- **Legacy:** "A good carpenter plants trees knowing he'll never see them grown."
- **Honor:** "My word is my contract. My work is my signature."

**Bonds:**
- His apprentices (currently training 6 young carpenters)
- The forest and sustainable practices
- His grandfather's axe (family heirloom for 150 years)
- The Oakenheart community
- His workshop (contains lifetime of tools and templates)
- His daughter Mira (learning the trade)

**Flaws:**
- Perfectionist to a fault (projects take longer than necessary)
- Stubborn about "the right way" to build things
- Holds grudge against merchant who wanted to clear-cut forest
- Sometimes values craftsmanship over people's urgent needs
- Struggles to say no to requests for free work
- Guilty about accident where apprentice lost finger

### Background & History
Aldric's family has been woodworkers for ten generations, but he's the first to achieve true mastery. His joints are invisible, his carvings lifelike, his furniture sold to royalty across both continents. He's transformed the family workshop into a renowned atelier.

He discovered his exceptional talent young—he could see how wood wanted to be shaped, could sense the grain and flow of lumber as clearly as others see color. By thirty, he was taking commissions from nobles. By fifty, he was turning them away—there's only so much he can produce, and he chooses projects that interest him.

He's gentle and patient, more interested in teaching than fame. He takes one apprentice at a time, training them for seven years before pronouncing them ready. His former students are among the finest woodworkers in the world.

### Connections
- **Workshop:** Master's Atelier in Silverpine
- **Apprentice:** Current apprentice nearing completion
- **Former Students:** Seventeen master craftspeople across the continent
- **Client:** Nobility and wealthy merchants
- **Supplier:** Various lumber operations, one special source


{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Special Source:** Gets exceptional wood from a dryad grove. They trade for his silence about their location.
2. **The Magical Technique:** His work involves minor nature magic he's never revealed. Not quite cheating, but not purely mundane.
3. **The Rejected Commission:** Once turned down a commission from someone important. They've been petty about it.
4. **The Masterwork Hidden:** Has created his greatest piece but keeps it hidden. Not for sale at any price.
5. **The Failing Eyes:** His sight is slowly deteriorating. Terrified of losing his gift.
}}
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Dryad Problem:** The dryad grove is threatened. Needs help without revealing their location.
2. **The Commission Conflict:** The rejected client is causing trouble. Needs diplomatic intervention.
3. **The Sight Quest:** Looking for magical solutions to his failing eyes. Discrete inquiries.
4. **The Apprentice Test:** His current apprentice needs a final test. Involves the party somehow.
5. **The Masterwork Viewing:** Might show his hidden masterwork to those who prove worthy.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Runs hand along wood grain while thinking
- Quotes "Grandfather Woodwise always said..."
- Makes small carved gifts during conversations
- Taps roof beams and posts to test them
- Carries chunk of wood to whittle
- Always smells sawdust on the air
- Gives structural advice even when not asked

**Key Details:**
- Trained by grandfather, legendary carpenter
- Leads guild of 30 carpenters in Oakenheart
- Developed sustainable forestry pact with druids
- Built half the town's current structures
- Teaches forestry and carpentry to anyone willing to learn
- Maintains strategic timber reserves (hidden location)
- Personal friend of Elder Thalindra (she trusts his forest practices)

{{monster,frame,wide
## Miller Tobias Waterwheel
*Medium humanoid (human), neutral good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 13 (padded armor)
**Hit Points** :: 52 (7d8 + 21)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Miller Tobias Waterwheel](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-miller-tobias-waterwheel.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 14 (+2) | 12 (+1) | 16 (+3) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 13 (+1) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Constitution +5, Intelligence +5
**Skills** :: Investigation +5, Nature +4, Perception +4, Tinker's Tools +7 (expertise), Engineer's Tools +7 (expertise), Insight +4
**Senses** :: Passive Perception 14
**Languages** :: Common, Dwarvish (engineering terms)
**Challenge** :: 4 (1,100 XP)
___
***Master Engineer.*** :: Has advantage on all checks related to mechanical devices, water systems, mills, or engineering problems. Can identify mechanical issues by sound or vibration.
***Hydraulic Expertise.*** :: Understands water flow, pressure, and mechanical advantage. Can calculate optimal wheel designs, water speeds, and power outputs.
***Jury Rigger.*** :: Given basic tools and materials, can temporarily repair almost any mechanical device. Repairs last 24 hours before needing proper maintenance.
***Powder Knowledge.*** :: Has extensive experience with grain dust explosions and fire prevention. Knows how to prevent or cause explosive conditions.
***Precise Calculations.*** :: Can mentally calculate weights, volumes, ratios, and mechanical advantages with perfect accuracy. Never makes math errors.
***Tinkerer's Eye.*** :: Can assess the quality and value of any mechanical device at a glance. Knows if something is well-made, defective, or sabotaged.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with his Heavy Wrench or Grain Sack.
***Heavy Wrench.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d8+2 bludgeoning damage.::
***Special.*** :: On hit, can attempt to disarm target if they're wielding a mechanical or metal weapon (contested Athletics check).
***Grain Sack.*** :: Improvised Weapon: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d6+2 bludgeoning damage.
***Special.*** :: On hit, target must succeed DC 13 Strength save or be knocked prone (40 lbs of grain is heavy).
***Mechanical Trap (Preparation Required).*** :: Given 10 minutes, can rig a mechanical trap using mill equipment. Examples:
- Swinging beam (DC 13 Dex save, 2d10 bludgeoning)
- Grain avalanche (20-ft cone, DC 13 Str save, 3d6 bludgeoning + buried)
- Millstone drop (30-ft area, DC 14 Dex save, 4d10 bludgeoning + prone)
***Sabotage Detection (1/Day).*** :: Examines mechanical device and instantly knows if it's been tampered with, how, and approximately when.
### Reactions
***Deflect Machinery.*** :: When a mechanical device attacks him or an ally within 5 ft., can use reaction to jam it with a tool. Device malfunctions and misses its attack.
***Practical Knowledge.*** :: When an ally within 30 ft. makes an Intelligence check related to mechanics or engineering, can provide guidance granting advantage on the check.
*"The mill turns day and night, just like the world. We feed the wheel, the wheel feeds us."*
}}

### Physical Description
Average height (5'10", 180 lbs) but powerfully built from years of hauling grain sacks and working machinery. Flour dust permanently stains his clothes and hair white, making him look older. Practical brown work clothes always covered in flour. Strong hands with blacksmith-like grip strength. Brown eyes that constantly assess mechanical workings. Short practical hair usually white with flour. Clean-shaven face dusted with flour. Smells of fresh flour, water, and machine oil. Moves with efficiency of someone used to dangerous machinery.

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Padded Leather Apron (AC 11, protects against flour dust, sparks)
- **Primary Tool:** Heavy Wrench (2 ft. long, masterwork, doubles as weapon)
- **Tools:** Tinker's tools, engineer's tools (both masterwork quality)
- **Belt:** Tool belt with hammers, pliers, oil can, measuring tape
- **Knife:** Utility knife (1d4 damage, for cutting rope/sacks)
- **Lantern:** Hooded lantern (essential in mill work, oil flask)
- **Other:** Chalk for marking, leather gloves, safety goggles (dwarven made)
- **Emergency:** Length of rope, pulleys, spare gears

### Personality
Traits
- Constantly wipes flour off clothes (futile habit)
- Explains things using mill and water metaphors
- Listens to machine sounds to diagnose problems
- Practical and direct in speech
- Takes pride in the quality of ground flour
- Patient with questions, impatient with incompetence
- Always knows what time it is by mill wheel rotations

**Ideals:**
- **Precision:** "Flour quality depends on perfect millstone gaps. Life's the same—precision matters."
- **Service:** "Every loaf of bread starts here. That's responsibility."
- **Innovation:** "There's always a better wheel design. Always room to improve."
- **Reliability:** "The mill runs 24 hours because people rely on it. So do I."

**Bonds:**
- His watermill (built it himself 20 years ago)
- The town of Willowbrook (feeds them all)
- His apprentice Jonas (teaching him the trade)
- The river (source of his power and livelihood)
- His late wife's memory (she designed the wheel)
- The mechanical innovation he's working on

**Flaws:**
- Obsessive about mill maintenance (checks it hourly)
- Fears fire above all else (grain dust explosions)
- Guilty about profiting when grain prices rise during famine
- Distrusts magic (prefers mechanical solutions)
- Sometimes ignores family for mill work
- Paranoid about sabotage after previous incident

### Background & History
The Waterwheel mill has ground grain for the village of Millbrook for two hundred years. Tobias is the fifth generation to run it, and possibly the last—his sons have left for city trades, and his daughter shows no interest in flour-dusted labor.

He's content with his life: steady work, respected position, enough coin to be comfortable. He knows every farmer within ten miles, their crops, their troubles, their secrets. The mill is where people talk while waiting for their grain, and Tobias listens more than he speaks.

But lately, something is wrong with the river. Fish are dying, the water tastes strange, and the wheel has been harder to turn. Tobias has been investigating quietly, and what he's found frightens him.

### Connections
- **Community:** Millbrook village (300 residents)
- **Customers:** Every farm within ten miles
- **Daughter:** Sarah Waterwheel (herbalist, lives in town)
- **Friend:** Forester Galen Sustainharvest (shares concerns about the land)
- **Worry:** Whatever is poisoning the river

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Upstream Source:** Has traced the river pollution to an abandoned mine. Something is leaking from it.
2. **The Listening Ear:** Knows secrets about half the valley from mill conversations. Never tells.
3. **The Hidden Fortune:** Has more saved than anyone suspects. Waiting to see if his daughter needs it.
4. **The Old Tunnels:** The mill basement connects to tunnels that lead... somewhere. Never explored far.
5. **The War Past:** Served as a soldier in his youth. Killed people. Became a miller partly to atone.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The River Investigation:** Needs help investigating the abandoned mine safely.
2. **The Tunnel Mystery:** Strange sounds from the basement tunnels. Needs someone to explore.
3. **The Secret Keeper:** Has information the party needs. Might share if asked right.
4. **The Daughter's Trouble:** Sarah is in some kind of difficulty. Needs discrete help.
5. **The Mill Defense:** Something is threatening the mill. Needs capable fighters.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Constantly wipes flour from hands
- Checks pocket watch obsessively
- Taps rhythm of mill wheel on tables
- Explains everything with water flow analogies
- Offers fresh bread to visitors
- Mutters calculations under breath
- Always coated in fine white flour dust

**Key Details:**
- Owns and operates Willowbrook's primary grain mill
- Processes grain for 20 miles around
- Designed revolutionary waterwheel that's 30% more efficient
- Dwarven engineers study his wheel design
- Supplies flour to both kingdoms
- Maintains strategic grain reserves during harvest
- His mill is local news center (everyone visits)

{{monster,frame,wide
## Lady Seraphina Riverbrook
*Medium humanoid (human), lawful neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (studded leather + Dex)
**Hit Points** :: 72 (11d8 + 22)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Lady Seraphina Riverbrook](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-lady-seraphina-riverbrook.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 12 (+1) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 18 (+4) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Dexterity +6, Wisdom +5, Charisma +7
**Skills** :: Deception +7, History +6, Insight +8 (expertise), Intimidation +7, Perception +5, Persuasion +10 (expertise), Rapier +6
**Senses** :: Passive Perception 15
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Infernal (business contracts), Sylvan
**Challenge** :: 6 (2,300 XP)
___
***Noble Authority.*** :: Has advantage on Charisma checks when dealing with commoners, merchants, or lower nobility. Can invoke noble privilege to access restricted areas or demand audience with officials.
***Diplomatic Immunity.*** :: In civilized areas, attacking her openly brings serious legal consequences. She can parley even with hostile forces (though this doesn't guarantee safety).
***Resource Management.*** :: Has extensive knowledge of land management, water rights, taxation, agriculture, and resource allocation. Can assess land value, crop yields, and economic viability at a glance.
***Legal Expert.*** :: Knows noble law, land rights, contract law, and water rights extensively. Can craft ironclad contracts or find loopholes in existing ones.
***Dueling Training.*** :: Trained in noble fencing arts. Has advantage on Initiative and attack rolls when fighting one-on-one honorable duels.
***Political Network.*** :: Maintains relationships with nobility across both kingdoms. Can send messages and gather information through her network (takes 1-3 days depending on distance).
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with her Rapier or one rapier attack and uses Commanding Presence.
***Riverbrook Rapier +1.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d8+4 piercing damage.::
***Special.*** :: Family heirloom blade. On critical hit, target must succeed DC 15 Constitution save or be poisoned for 1 minute (blade is enchanted with subtle venom coating that replenishes daily).
***Elegant Riposte (Recharge 5-6).*** :: When a creature misses her with a melee attack, she immediately counterattacks. +7 to hit, 2d8+4 piercing damage.
***Main Gauche.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d4+3 piercing damage.::
***Special.*** :: Used for parrying. See reactions.
***Commanding Presence.*** :: Target one creature within 30 ft. that can hear and understand her. Target must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or be charmed or frightened (her choice) for 1 minute. On successful save, immune for 24 hours.
***Demand Negotiation (1/Day).*** :: Forces a pause in combat if at least one enemy can be reasoned with. All combatants must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or be compelled to hear her out for 1 minute. Attacking her during this time breaks the effect.
### Reactions
***Parry.*** :: When attacked with a melee weapon, adds +3 AC against that attack using her main gauche. If this causes the attack to miss, she can immediately riposte (no action cost, +6 to hit, 1d8+3 damage).
***Political Leverage.*** :: When threatened, can invoke her noble connections. Attackers must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or hesitate (disadvantage on their next attack). Only works once per encounter per enemy.
*"Land ownership is a sacred trust. We do not own the earth; we are merely its temporary stewards."*
}}

### Physical Description
Elegant and commanding presence (5'8", 145 lbs) with the poise of generations of nobility. Auburn hair worn in practical noble style, sometimes covered with silk scarf. Striking green eyes that assess people instantly. Fair skin despite outdoor work managing estates. Wears practical but expensive clothing—reinforced silk that looks decorative but allows movement. Always carries rapier at hip, though she makes it look decorative. Moves with fencer's grace. Smells of rose water and parchment. Hands show evidence of both sword practice and ledger work.

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Fine Studded Leather (AC 14, disguised as fashionable clothing)
- **Primary Weapon:** Riverbrook Rapier +1 (family heirloom, magically keen)
- **Secondary:** Main Gauche (parrying dagger, masterwork)
- **Clothing:** Noble's traveling outfit (worth 50 gp, reinforced silk)
- **Jewelry:** Signet ring (family crest, proves identity), pearl necklace (worth 500 gp)
- **Documents:** Leather portfolio with land deeds, contracts, maps
- **Tools:** Wax seal, noble stationery, ledger books
- **Emergency:** Hidden lockbox key (opens vault in Kaer Thandros)
- **Potions:** 2 potions of healing, 1 potion of water breathing (insurance)
- **Mount:** Well-bred riding horse (outside), saddle and tack

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks with clear authority, expects to be obeyed
- Listens intently to all sides before deciding
- Uses legal terminology in casual conversation
- Taps fingers when calculating costs/benefits
- Maintains perfect posture always
- Treats commoners with respect (unusual for nobility)
- Quick to correct contract errors or unfair deals

**Ideals:**
- **Justice:** "Law must protect both the powerful and the powerless, or it protects no one."
- **Stewardship:** "This land will outlast me. I must leave it better than I found it."
- **Honor:** "My word is my bond. Once given, I do not break it."
- **Balance:** "The river must flow for the miller and the farmer both."

**Bonds:**
- Her family estate (Riverbrook Manor, 500 acres)
- The people living on her lands (300+ tenants)
- Her deceased father's legacy (trying to honor)
- The Riverbrook family name (ancient lineage)
- Her younger brother Marcus (captain in the army)
- The river itself (family named for it)

**Flaws:**
- Stubborn about family honor and tradition
- Struggles to trust after betrayal by former steward
- Sometimes prioritizes law over people's immediate needs
- Guilty about living in wealth while tenants struggle
- Fears becoming cruel like other nobles
- Duty-bound to arranged marriage she doesn't want

### Background & History
Seraphina was born to wealth and privilege, the only daughter of Lord Riverbrook. She was expected to marry well and manage a noble household. Instead, she discovered a passion for governance, studying law and administration while her father prepared her for a political marriage.

When her father died unexpectedly, she had to fight to inherit—the law was unclear, and cousins contested her claim. She won through a combination of legal brilliance and strategic marriage to a lower noble who was content to let her rule. She's been Lady of Riverbrook for fifteen years.

She's transformed her domain into a model of efficient governance: roads maintained, justice fair, taxes reasonable. Other nobles either admire or resent her success. She's ambitious but patient, building alliances for a long-term goal she rarely discusses.

### Connections
- **Domain:** Riverbrook territory (12,000 residents)
- **Husband:** Lord Gareth Riverbrook (supportive, handles military)
- **Rival:** Lord Aldris Goldshore (political opponent)
- **Ally:** Various reform-minded nobles
- **Goal:** The High Council seat

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Council Ambition:** Working toward a seat on the High Council. Would be the first woman in three generations.
2. **The Marriage Arrangement:** Her marriage is purely political. Gareth prefers men; they're friends, not lovers.
3. **The Cousin Problem:** The cousin who contested her inheritance hasn't given up. She's watching him.
4. **The Adopted Heir:** Secretly looking to adopt an heir since she and Gareth will have no children.
5. **The Information Network:** Has built an intelligence network to rival any spy master's.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Political Alliance:** Offers the party patronage in exchange for services.
2. **The Cousin Crisis:** The cousin is making moves. Needs investigation or counteraction.
3. **The Heir Search:** Looking for the right person to adopt. Might test party members.
4. **The Reform Proposal:** Working on major governance reform. Needs allies to push it through.
5. **The Intelligence Trade:** Has information the party needs. Willing to trade.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Stands straight, shoulders back, even when tired
- Makes eye contact that forces honesty
- Uses "we" when speaking about estate matters
- Quotes father: "Father always said..."
- Signs documents with elaborate flourish
- Touches rapier hilt when threatened
- Speaks firmly but never shouts

**Key Details:**
- Controls water rights for 50-mile section of river
- Manages 500-acre estate with 300+ tenant farmers
- Mediates land disputes between nobles and commoners
- Trained in swordplay since childhood (family tradition)
- Opposed to her family's arranged marriage plan
- Advocates for tenant farmers' rights (controversial)
- Secretly funding irrigation projects from personal wealth
- Has veto power over water use decisions

{{monster,frame,wide
## Captain Marcus Frontiersman (Werewolf)
*Medium humanoid (human, shapechanger), chaotic good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 17 (half-plate)
**Hit Points** :: 112 (14d10 + 42)
**Speed** :: 30 ft. (40 ft. in hybrid or wolf form)
![Captain Marcus Frontiersman](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-captain-marcus-frontiersman.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 12 (+1) | 14 (+2) | 15 (+2) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +7, Constitution +6, Wisdom +5
**Skills** :: Athletics +7, Insight +5, Intimidation +5, Perception +5, Survival +8 (expertise)
**Damage Immunities** :: Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from nonmagical attacks not made with silvered weapons (in hybrid or wolf form)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft. (in wolf or hybrid form), Passive Perception 15
**Languages** :: Common, Frontier dialect
**Challenge** :: 8 (3,900 XP)
___
***Shapechanger.*** :: Can use an action to polymorph into a wolf-humanoid hybrid or into a Large wolf, or back into human form. Statistics are the same in each form, except as noted. Equipment melds into new form. Reverts to human if reduced to 0 HP.
***Keen Hearing and Smell.*** :: Has advantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks that rely on hearing or smell (in wolf or hybrid form).
***Pack Tactics.*** :: Has advantage on attack rolls against a creature if at least one ally is within 5 ft. of the creature and isn't incapacitated.
***Lycanthropy Control (Partial).*** :: Can resist transformation during normal full moons with DC 15 Wisdom save. On failure, transforms and retains vague awareness but is aggressive. Always transforms during blood moons (no save).
***Silver Vulnerability.*** :: Takes normal damage from silvered weapons (bypasses immunity).
***Military Tactician.*** :: Grants +2 to initiative rolls for all allies within 30 ft. Can use bonus action to grant ally advantage on their next attack.
***Frontier Survival Expert.*** :: Has advantage on Survival checks in wilderness. Cannot become lost in natural terrain.
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes three attacks with longsword or two with longbow.
***Longsword +1.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 1d8+5 slashing damage (1d10+5 versatile).
***Longbow.*** :: Ranged Weapon Attack: +5 to hit, range 150/600 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 1d8+2 piercing damage.
***Leadership (Recharge 5-6).*** :: For 1 minute, all allies within 30 ft. gain +1 to attack rolls and saving throws.
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes one bite attack and two claw attacks, or three claw attacks.
***Bite.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 1d8+4 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 14 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy.
***Claw.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 2d4+4 slashing damage.
***Longsword +1 (Two-Handed).*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 1d10+5 slashing damage. (Can wield weapons in hybrid form with difficulty)
***Howl of the Hunt (1/Day).*** :: Releases a terrifying howl. All creatures within 60 ft. that can hear must succeed DC 14 Wisdom save or be frightened for 1 minute. Allies gain advantage on their next attack.
***Bite.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 2d6+4 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 14 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy.
***Pounce.*** :: If the wolf moves at least 20 ft. straight toward a creature and hits with bite, target must succeed DC 14 Strength save or be knocked prone. If prone, wolf can make another bite attack as bonus action.
### Actions
***Protective Transformation.*** :: When ally within 10 ft. is attacked by creature that would kill them, Marcus can transform into hybrid form as reaction and intercept the attack (becomes new target).
***Silver Sensitivity.*** :: If hit by silvered weapon, must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or revert to human form immediately.
### Reactions
***Protective Transformation.*** :: When ally within 10 ft. is attacked by creature that would kill them, Marcus can transform into hybrid form as reaction and intercept the attack (becomes new target).
***Silver Sensitivity.*** :: If hit by silvered weapon, must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or revert to human form immediately.
*"I protect this frontier from monsters. The irony isn't lost on me."*
}}

### Physical Description
(Human Form)
Rugged and battle-hardened (6'1", 200 lbs) with the weathered look of frontier life. Dark brown hair kept military short. Intense gray eyes that sometimes flash amber in moonlight. Strong jawline with short beard showing early gray. Multiple scars across face and arms from frontier combat. Moves with controlled power, like a caged wolf. Wears half-plate that's seen heavy use but is meticulously maintained. Smells of leather, steel, and wild places. Carries himself with authority but growing weariness.

**(Hybrid Form):** Gains wolf-like features—elongated snout, fangs, claws, fur covering body, digitigrade legs, tail. Height increases to 7 feet. Eyes glow amber. Still recognizable but terrifying. Retains ability to speak (with difficulty).

**(Wolf Form):** Large black wolf with gray eyes. Indistinguishable from dire wolf except for amber eye-flash in moonlight.

### Equipment
(Human Form)
- **Armor:** Half-Plate +1 (custom-fitted, reinforced)
- **Primary Weapon:** Longsword +1 "Frontier's Edge" (silvered, ironically)
- **Secondary:** Silvered Dagger (keeps it as test of control)
- **Ranged:** Longbow with 40 arrows (20 normal, 20 silvered)
- **Shield:** Heater Shield (+2 AC when used)
- **Cloak:** Frontier Captain's Cloak (marks authority, grants +1 to Charisma checks with frontier folk)
- **Amulet:** Moonstone Pendant (helps resist transformations, grants +2 to Wisdom saves vs. lycanthropy)
- **Belt:** Utility belt with rope, signal horn, rations, waterskin
- **Potions:** 3 potions of healing, 1 potion of heroism
- **Special:** Silver chain (last resort restraint if he loses control)
- **Documents:** Captain's commission, frontier maps, wanted posters

### Personality
Traits
- Constantly aware of moon phases
- Checks silver weapons compulsively
- Keeps distance from people he cares about
- Patrols alone whenever possible
- Drinks wolfsbane tea nightly (bitter, helps control)
- Watches his hands for signs of transformation
- Protective of others to extreme degree

**Ideals:**
- **Protection:** "These people need a guardian, even if that guardian is cursed."
- **Control:** "I will master this curse or die trying. I will not endanger innocents."
- **Duty:** "I swore an oath to protect this frontier. The curse doesn't change that."
- **Redemption:** "Maybe by protecting others, I can atone for what I've become."

**Bonds:**
- His frontier militia (30 volunteers he commands)
- Westmarch settlement (200 people relying on his protection)
- Lady Seraphina Riverbrook (secret love, fears revealing curse)
- His late mentor Captain Aldric (infected him while dying)
- The memory of his first kill as a werewolf (still haunts him)
- His younger sister in Silverpine (hasn't seen her in 2 years)

**Flaws:**
- Increasingly isolated, pushes people away
- Guilty about curse transmission (has accidentally infected two people)
- Suicidal thoughts during full moons (considers silver to the heart)
- Drinks heavily to cope with curse
- Refuses magical help (fears making it worse)
- Doesn't sleep well (nightmares of transformation kills)
- Secret meetings with The Silver Wolf (who understands)

### Background & History
Marcus was a promising young captain in the border guard when the werewolf pack attacked. Most of his patrol died; he was bitten and left for dead. He survived, changed, and faced a choice: surrender to the beast or master it.

Twenty years later, he's done the impossible—maintained his humanity while using his lycanthropy to protect the frontier. The wild lands are full of creatures that normal soldiers can't fight; Marcus can. He operates alone, reporting to commanders who officially don't know what he is.

He's not cured—there's no cure. But he's found equilibrium: running wild during full moons in unpopulated areas, taking wolfsbane to maintain control, and channeling the predator inside toward protecting the helpless. It costs him everything else. He has no family, few friends, and no hope of a normal life.

### Connections
- **Chain of Command:** Reports to Commander Kael Stormwatcher (knows the truth)
- **Pack:** The Silver Wolf (complicated)
- **Ally:** Hermit Sage Morganna Whisperwind (provides wolfsbane)
- **Enemy:** The werewolf pack that turned him (still hunting them)
- **Self:** The beast within

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Pack Hunt:** Has been systematically hunting the werewolves who turned him. Three left.
2. **The Control Secret:** His control isn't natural—it's a ritual Morganna developed. Requires monthly renewal.
3. **The Bite Risk:** Has accidentally bitten two people. Found them and ensured they received help.
4. **The Retirement Dream:** Wants to find a cure and live normally. Knows it probably doesn't exist.
5. **The Silver Wolf Connection:** The Silver Wolf is his turned mentor. They're linked but on opposite paths.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Hunt Continues:** Has located another werewolf from the original pack. Needs help taking it down.
2. **The Control Crisis:** Something is interfering with his control ritual. Needs investigation.
3. **The New Victim:** Someone has been bitten. He needs help getting them to Morganna.
4. **The Silver Wolf Conflict:** The confrontation with his mentor is coming. Needs allies.
5. **The Cure Rumor:** Heard of a possible cure. Needs someone to investigate while he stays hidden.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Touches moonstone amulet when stressed
- Checks moon phase calendar constantly
- Refuses to eat rare meat (reminds him of curse)
- Volunteers for dangerous missions (death wish)
- Growls unconsciously when angry
- Sniffs air when suspicious (hybrid sense memory)
- Keeps silver dagger visible (warning to himself)

**Key Details:**
- Commands Westmarch frontier garrison (30 militia)
- Infected with lycanthropy 3 years ago
- Has partial control during most full moons
- Secretly meets Silver Wolf for advice/support
- In love with Lady Seraphina Riverbrook (terrified to tell her)
- Has infected 2 people accidentally (deep guilt)
- Considers suicide regularly but duty prevents it
- Knows Elder Thalindra suspects his curse
