## The Silver Wolf
*Medium humanoid (human, shapechanger), chaotic neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 18 (natural armor in hybrid form)
**Hit Points** :: 142 (17d10 + 51)
**Speed** :: 40 ft. (50 ft. in hybrid or wolf form)
![The Silver Wolf](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-the-silver-wolf.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 20 (+5) | 16 (+3) | 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 12 (+1) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +9, Dexterity +7, Constitution +8, Wisdom +7
**Skills** :: Acrobatics +7, Athletics +9, Intimidation +5, Perception +11 (expertise), Stealth +11 (expertise), Survival +11 (expertise)
**Damage Immunities** :: Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from nonmagical attacks not made with silvered weapons
**Senses** :: Darkvision 120 ft., Blindsight 30 ft. (hearing/smell based), Passive Perception 21
**Languages** :: Common, Sylvan, understands Druidic
**Challenge** :: 10 (5,900 XP)
___
***Shapechanger (Master).*** :: Can transform between human, hybrid, and wolf forms as a bonus action. Can maintain hybrid form indefinitely. Has complete control during all moon phases.
***Perfect Control.*** :: Immune to forced transformations. Never loses control to beast instincts. Can voluntarily fail saves to resist transformation if desired.
***Keen Senses (All Forms).*** :: Advantage on Perception checks using hearing or smell. Can track by scent alone, identifying individual scents up to 24 hours old.
***Pack Lord.*** :: Other lycanthropes view him with respect/fear. Has advantage on Charisma checks with lycanthropes. Can sense other lycanthropes within 100 ft.
***Regeneration.*** :: Regains 10 HP at start of his turn if he has at least 1 HP. Doesn't regenerate damage from silvered weapons.
***Legendary Resistance (2/Day).*** :: If fails saving throw, can choose to succeed instead.
***Moon-Blessed.*** :: During full moons, gains +2 to all ability scores and his regeneration increases to 15 HP per turn.
***Pack Tactics.*** :: Advantage on attack rolls against creatures if at least one ally is within 5 ft.
***Ambush Predator.*** :: Has advantage on attack rolls against creatures that haven't taken a turn in combat yet.
***Trackless.*** :: Leaves no trail in wilderness. Can't be tracked by normal means.
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes three unarmed strikes or weapon attacks.
***Unarmed Strike.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 1d6+5 bludgeoning damage.
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes one bite attack and three claw attacks.
***Bite.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 2d8+5 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 16 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy (but only if Aldren wishes it).
***Claw.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 2d6+5 slashing damage.
***Rending Claws.*** :: If both claw attacks hit same target, deal extra 3d6 slashing damage.
***Alpha's Howl (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Releases a primal howl. Effects depend on target:
***- Allied lycanthropes.*** :: Gain 20 temp HP, advantage on attacks for 1 minute
***- Enemies.*** :: DC 16 Wisdom save or frightened for 1 minute
***- Range.*** :: 300 ft.
***Pounce.*** :: If moves at least 20 ft. toward target and hits with claw, target must succeed DC 17 Strength save or be knocked prone. Can make bite attack as bonus action against prone targets.
***Savage Maul (Recharge 6).*** :: Focuses all attacks on single target. Makes four claw attacks. If two or more hit, also makes bite attack. If bite hits, deals double damage.
***Bite.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
***Hit.*** :: 3d8+5 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 16 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy (only if Aldren wishes).
***Pounce.*** :: If moves 30 ft. toward target and hits with bite, target must succeed DC 17 Strength save or be knocked prone. Can make another bite as bonus action.
***Pack Leader's Call (1/Day).*** :: Summons 2d4 wolves (CR 1/4 each) that arrive in 1d4 rounds and obey his commands for 1 hour.
### Actions
***Uncanny Dodge.*** :: When attacker he can see hits him with attack, can halve the damage.
***Savage Riposte.*** :: When creature misses him with melee attack, can immediately make claw attack against them.
***Protective Pounce.*** :: When ally within 30 ft. is attacked, can move up to half speed and impose disadvantage on attack roll.
### Reactions
***Uncanny Dodge.*** :: When attacker he can see hits him with attack, can halve the damage.
***Savage Riposte.*** :: When creature misses him with melee attack, can immediately make claw attack against them.
***Protective Pounce.*** :: When ally within 30 ft. is attacked, can move up to half speed and impose disadvantage on attack roll.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Move.** :: Moves up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
**Claw Attack.** :: Makes one claw attack.
**Detect (Costs 1).** :: Makes Perception check or senses all lycanthropes within 100 ft.
**Howl (Costs 2).** :: Uses Alpha's Howl if available.
**Transform (Costs 1).** :: Changes between forms.
*"The curse is not evil. The man makes that choice, not the beast."*
}}

### Physical Description
**(Human Form - Rarely Seen):**
Rugged and weathered (6'0", 190 lbs) with the look of someone who lives in wilderness. Prematurely gray hair worn long and wild. Piercing gray eyes that sometimes flash silver. Multiple scars across exposed skin. Strong build from years of hunting. Wears simple travel-worn clothes. Moves with predator's grace even in human form.

**(Hybrid Form - His Preferred State):**
Towering werewolf (7'5", 320 lbs) with silver-gray fur that seems to shimmer in moonlight. Powerful build with visible muscle definition. Elongated wolf snout with intelligent gray eyes. Large pointed ears constantly swiveling. Massive claws (6 inches long) and fangs. Digitigrade legs with powerful haunches. Long bushy tail. Wears the gray cloak like a badge. Despite terrifying appearance, moves with controlled grace.

**(Wolf Form - For Travel):**
Large silver-gray wolf (size of a small horse). Appears as a dire wolf but with distinctive silver sheen to fur. Gray eyes remain intelligent and aware. Faster than normal wolves. Often mistaken for spirit or fey wolf.

### Equipment
(Rarely Carries)
- **Clothing:** Simple traveler's clothes (human form), shreds when transforming
- **Amulet:** Silver moon pendant (proof he's mastered the curse, doesn't harm him)
- **Cloak:** Weather-worn gray cloak (wolf form can wear it like a cape)
- **Pouch:** Small leather pouch with herbs, wolfsbane antidote, emergency rations
- **No Weapons:** Relies entirely on natural weapons
- **No Armor:** Natural armor in hybrid form superior to any worn armor

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks little, observes much
- Comfortable in prolonged silences
- Refers to himself as "we" (human and beast are one)
- Watches moon phases but isn't controlled by them
- Protective of innocent lycanthropes struggling with curse
- Hunts those who abuse lycanthropy
- Smells everyone upon meeting (habit)

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Man and beast can coexist in one soul. The struggle creates strength."
- **Choice:** "The curse doesn't make monsters. People choose to be monsters."
- **Protection:** "Those who cannot control the beast need guidance, not execution."
- **Nature:** "The wild is not evil. Civilization fears what it doesn't understand."

**Bonds:**
- Lycanthropes struggling with control (mentors them)
- The forest and wild places (his true home)
- Captain Marcus Frontiersman (teaching him control)
- The memory of his pack (all dead now)
- An oath made long ago (won't speak of it)
- The balance between civilization and wilderness

**Flaws:**
- Increasingly isolated from humanity
- Sometimes forgets human social norms
- Violent toward anyone who abuses lycanthropy
- Guilty about past (killed people before gaining control)
- Fears complete loss of humanity despite control
- Refuses to fully commit to either beast or man
- Hunted by silver-armed hunters (constant vigilance)

### Background & History
Before the curse, she was Captain Helena Silverbane, the most decorated officer in the frontier guard. She was Marcus's mentor, the one who trained him, the one who led the patrol into the werewolf ambush. She was the first bitten, and the first to turn.

Unlike Marcus, she didn't fight the beast—she embraced it. The Wolf offered freedom from human frailty, from pain, from the slow decline of aging. She disappeared into the wilderness and built a pack of werewolves who live as she does: hunting, running, wild and free.

She's not evil in any simple sense. Her pack doesn't attack innocents unprovoked. But they are predators, and they claim hunting territories that sometimes conflict with human settlements. She believes lycanthropy is a gift and seeks to share it—willing or not—with those she deems worthy.

### Connections
- **Pack:** Twelve werewolves loyal to her
- **Former Protégé:** Captain Marcus Frontiersman (love and hate intertwined)
- **Enemy:** Werewolf hunters across the region
- **Ally:** Some fey creatures who appreciate her wildness
- **Target:** Soldiers and warriors she deems "worthy" of the gift

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Original Guilt:** She led the patrol into the ambush deliberately. Had already made a deal with the pack.
2. **The Marcus Obsession:** Wants Marcus to join her willingly. Has been slowly manipulating circumstances.
3. **The Fey Alliance:** Made deals with unseelie fey for territorial protection.
4. **The Pack Instability:** Some pack members are growing too wild. She's losing control.
5. **The Cure Fear:** Knows a cure exists. Terrified that if Marcus finds it, she'll want it too.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Pack Contact:** Reaches out to the party as neutral intermediaries.
2. **The Territory Dispute:** Her pack is encroaching on human lands. Negotiate or fight.
3. **The Cure Information:** Has information about a cure. Might trade it—for the right price.
4. **The Marcus Trap:** Has set a trap for Marcus. The party might be able to intervene.
5. **The Pack Rebellion:** Some werewolves have gone feral. She needs help stopping them before hunters blame her pack.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Sniffs air constantly
- Tilts head like a wolf when confused
- Growls low when threatened
- Uses minimal words, maximum meaning
- Makes eye contact that feels predatory
- Comfortable on all fours in hybrid form
- Howls at the moon (celebration, not compulsion)

**Speech Patterns:**
- "We smell fear on you. Unnecessary."
- "The moon calls. We answer freely."
- "Control comes from acceptance, not resistance."
- "Your beast and you are not enemies. Learn this."

## Forester Galen Sustainharvest
*Medium humanoid (half-elf), neutral good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (studded leather + Dex)
**Hit Points** :: 78 (12d8 + 24)
**Speed** :: 30 ft., climb 30 ft.

|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 14 (+2) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 14 (+2) | 18 (+4) | 13 (+1) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Strength +5, Dexterity +6, Wisdom +7
**Skills** :: Animal Handling +7, Athletics +5, Nature +8 (expertise), Perception +10 (expertise), Stealth +6, Survival +10 (expertise), Woodcarver's Tools +5
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 20
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Druidic (honorary), can speak with animals and plants
**Challenge** :: 6 (2,300 XP)
___
***Fey Ancestry.*** :: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
***Trance.*** :: Meditates 4 hours instead of sleeping.
***Favored Enemy (Aberrations, Undead).*** :: +2 damage against these creature types. Advantage on tracking them and Intelligence checks to recall information about them.
***Natural Explorer (Forest).*** :: In forest terrain:
***Spellcasting.*** :: 8th-level ranger. Spell save DC 15, +7 to hit with spell attacks.
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Cure Wounds, Entangle, Goodberry, Speak with Animals
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Pass without Trace, Spike Growth, Locate Plants or Animals
***Sustainable Forestry Expert.*** :: Can assess forest health, tree ages, and sustainable harvest rates with perfect accuracy. Knows exactly which trees can be safely harvested without damaging ecosystem.
***Tree Speaker.*** :: Can communicate with trees (as *speak with plants* spell) without expending spell slot. Trees willingly share information about recent events with him.
***Forest Network.*** :: Maintains relationships with druids, rangers, and forest spirits across 100-mile radius. Can send messages through the trees (takes 24 hours).
***Animal Companion - Moss the Bear.*** :: Always accompanied by an old brown bear (CR 1) that trusts him completely.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with Longbow or Handaxe, or three with Hunting Knife (melee).
***Forestkeeper's Longbow +1.*** :: Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, range 150/600 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d8+4 piercing damage plus 1d6 poison damage (arrows tipped with natural toxins).::
***Special.*** :: Can choose nonlethal damage. Poisoned creatures have disadvantage on Perception checks (toxin affects senses).
***Hunting Knife.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d6+3 piercing damage.::
***Handaxe +1.*** :: Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 20/60 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d6+4 slashing damage.::
***Entangling Roots (Recharge 5-6, replaces spell slot).*** :: Causes roots to erupt from ground in 20-foot radius centered on point within 60 ft. Creatures in area must succeed DC 15 Strength save or be restrained. Lasts 1 minute or until destroyed (AC 10, 20 HP per 10-foot square).
***Call Animal Ally (1/Day).*** :: Summons 1d4 forest animals (wolves, bears, boars, or elk) that arrive in 1d4 rounds and obey commands for 1 hour.
***Mark the Violator (1/Day).*** :: Marks creature that has harmed the forest unnecessarily. Marked creature:
- Has disadvantage on Stealth checks in forests
- Animals are hostile toward them
- Druids and rangers can sense the mark
- Lasts until they atone for the damage
### Reactions
***Forest's Warning.*** :: When ally within 30 ft. is about to trigger natural hazard (falling branch, hidden pit, dangerous plant), can shout warning granting +5 to their saving throw or check to avoid.
***Defensive Retreat.*** :: When hit by attack, can immediately move up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks (bonus action next turn)
.
*"Cut three, plant ten. That's how the forest survives, and so do we."*
}}
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Physical Description
Lean and weathered (5'11", 165 lbs) with the wiry build of someone who climbs and hikes constantly. Silver-streaked brown hair worn in practical ponytail. Kind hazel eyes that shift green in certain lights (elf heritage). Tanned, lined face marked by years of outdoor work. Moves with quiet grace through forests. Wears earth-tone clothes that blend perfectly with forest. Perpetually has leaves, moss, and bark pieces on his person. Smells of pine, earth, and leather. His hands are calloused but gentle. Usually accompanied by Moss, a large old brown bear.

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Reinforced Studded Leather +1 (forest camouflage pattern)
- **Primary Weapon:** Forestkeeper's Longbow +1 (carved with growth runes)
- **Arrows:** Quiver with 40 arrows (20 normal, 10 poisoned, 10 nonlethal blunt)
- **Secondary:** Handaxe +1 (doubles as tool and weapon)
- **Tool:** Hunting Knife (razor sharp, used for careful bark removal)
- **Tools:** Woodcarver's tools, forester's marking axe, measuring rope
- **Cloak:** Forest Green Cloak (grants advantage on Stealth in forest)
- **Boots:** Soft Leather Boots (no sound when walking, tracks minimal)
- **Pack:** Rope, climbing gear, tree-marking paint, seedling pouches
- **Book:** Comprehensive forestry journal (40 years of observations)
- **Companion:** Moss the Bear (old brown bear, best friend)
- **Seeds:** Pouches of various tree seeds (oak, pine, maple, etc.)

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks softly, rarely raises voice
- Often pauses to touch or examine trees
- Quotes forest wisdom and old sayings
- Patient to extreme degree
- Treats trees like old friends
- Gentle but firm about forest protection
- Makes decisions slowly but confidently

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Take what you need, not what you want. Plant more than you harvest."
- **Wisdom:** "The forest teaches if you're patient enough to listen."
- **Stewardship:** "We don't own the forest. We serve it, and it serves us."
- **Future:** "I plant trees knowing I won't see them grown. That's the responsibility."

**Bonds:**
- The forest (considers it alive and conscious)
- His bear companion Moss (20 years together)
- Apprentice foresters he's training (12 current students)
- The druid circle (honorary member despite not being druid)
- His children and grandchildren (family of foresters)
- The memory of ancient trees he's lost

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes prioritizes trees over people
- Holds decades-long grudges against those who harmed forests
- Difficulty adapting to rapid change
- Guilty about trees felled under his authority
- Can't walk past sick tree without stopping to help
- Increasingly tired (age catching up)

### Background & History
Galen's family has managed this section of forest for twelve generations, carefully harvesting timber while maintaining the woodland's health. He learned the craft from his father, who learned from his father, an unbroken chain of knowledge stretching back centuries.

He's developed sustainable harvesting to a science: which trees to cut, which to preserve, how to encourage regrowth, when to let areas lie fallow. His forest produces steady timber while remaining healthy. Other foresters study his methods; lumber companies resent his restrictions.

Recently, he's noticed troubling changes. Trees are growing strangely, animals behaving oddly, and the forest's... feeling has shifted. Something is wrong at a level he can't quite identify, and it frightens him.

### Connections
- **Territory:** Three thousand acres of managed forest
- **Ally:** Miller Tobias Waterwheel (shares concerns)
- **Enemy:** Quickcut Lumber Company (wants his land)
- **Contact:** Druid Thornwood (magical advisor)
- **Family:** Wife and three children, all learning forestry

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Blight Signs:** Has seen early signs of magical blight. Not sure what to do about it.
2. **The Buried Thing:** Found something buried in a clearing. Ancient, magical, and getting warmer.
3. **The Lumber Company:** They've tried bribing, threatening, and sabotaging him. He has evidence.
4. **The Family Gift:** His family has minor forest magic. Nothing dramatic, just an affinity.
5. **The Evacuation Plan:** If things get bad enough, he knows how to get his family out fast.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Blight Investigation:** Needs magical help understanding what's happening to the forest.
2. **The Buried Discovery:** The thing in the clearing is definitely waking up. Needs excavation.
3. **The Lumber Fight:** Ready to move against Quickcut. Needs allies and legal help.
4. **The Forest Defense:** Something is coming. Needs help preparing.
5. **The Knowledge Share:** Willing to teach sustainable forestry to those who'll use it.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Runs hand along tree bark while talking
- Moss the bear is always nearby
- Knows every tree in hundred-mile radius by sight
- Offers fresh fruit from "forest gifts"
- Refers to trees by personality ("Old Grandfather Oak")
- Stops conversations to listen to forest sounds
- Makes gifts from carved wood

**Key Details:**
- 40+ years experience in sustainable forestry
- Honorary druid circle member (respects their teachings)
- Mediates between loggers and druids
- Trained 50+ foresters across his career
- Maintains seedling nursery (thousands of saplings)
- Maps every tree in managed territory
- Personal friend of Druid Thornwood
- Moss the bear saved his life 20 years ago

## Druid Thornwood
*Medium humanoid (firbolg), neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 16 (barkskin)
**Hit Points** :: 127 (15d8 + 60)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Druid Thornwood](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-druid-thornwood.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) | 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) | 20 (+5) | 14 (+2) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +6, Wisdom +9, Charisma +6
**Skills** :: Animal Handling +9, Arcana +6, Insight +9, Medicine +9, Nature +10 (expertise), Perception +9, Survival +9
**Damage Resistances** :: Poison
**Condition Immunities** :: Charmed, Frightened (while in forest)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 19, Tremorsense 30 ft. (through roots)
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Druidic, Giant, Primordial, can speak with beasts and plants
**Challenge** :: 11 (7,200 XP)
___
***Spellcasting.*** :: 12th-level druid (Circle of the Land - Forest). Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks.
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Druidcraft, Guidance, Produce Flame, Thorn Whip, Shillelagh
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Cure Wounds, Entangle, Goodberry, Speak with Animals
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Barkskin*, Hold Person, Pass without Trace, Spike Growth
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Call Lightning, Conjure Animals, Plant Growth, Speak with Plants
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Blight, Dominate Beast, Grasping Vine, Stone Shape
***5th level (2 slots).*** :: Commune with Nature, Cone of Cold (forest feature), Tree Stride
***6th level (1 slot).*** :: Transport via Plants, Wall of Thorns
***Forest Sanctuary.*** :: When a beast or plant creature attempts to attack him, must succeed DC 17 Wisdom save. On failure, must choose different target or action wasted. On success, immune for 24 hours.
***Wild Shape (2/Short Rest).*** :: Can wild shape into beasts up to CR 1 as action (swim speed at 8th level). Prefers brown bear, dire wolf, or giant eagle forms. Lasts 6 hours.
***Land's Stride.*** :: Moving through difficult terrain costs no extra movement. Can pass through magical plants without being slowed or taking damage.
***Nature's Ward.*** :: Immune to poison and disease. Can't be charmed or frightened by fey or plants.
***Root Network.*** :: While in forest, can sense disturbances through root systems within 300 ft. radius. Knows if creatures are moving through his territory.
***Thornwood Transformation (1/Day).*** :: For 10 minutes, becomes avatar of forest fury:
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with Thornwood Staff or casts a cantrip and makes one staff attack.
***Thornwood Staff (Shillelagh).*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 2d8+5 magical bludgeoning damage plus 1d8 poison damage (thorns).::
***Special.*** :: Staff regrows thorns naturally. On critical hit, target is grappled by thorny vines (escape DC 17).
***Thorn Whip.*** :: Ranged Spell Attack: +9 to hit, range 30 ft., one creature. ***Hit.*** 3d6 piercing damage and pull target 10 ft. closer.::
***Flame Seed (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Hurls explosive acorn. Ranged Spell Attack: +9 to hit, range 60 ft. ***Hit.*** 4d8 fire damage to target and 2d8 fire to all creatures within 5 ft. (Dex DC 17 half).::
***Command Forest (1/Day).*** :: In 60-foot radius, causes:
- All plants become difficult terrain for enemies
- Trees attempt to restrain enemies (DC 17 Str save or restrained)
- Party gains half cover from foliage
- Lasts 10 minutes
***Summon Forest Guardian (1/Day).*** :: Summons awakened tree (CR 2) that fights for 1 hour.
### Reactions
***Bramble Defense.*** :: When hit by melee attack, thorny brambles lash out at attacker. +9 to hit, 2d8 piercing damage.
***Nature's Intervention.*** :: When ally within 30 ft. takes damage, can cause vines to absorb some impact, reducing damage by 2d10+5.
***Root Trip.*** :: When creature within 10 ft. moves, can cause roots to trip them. DC 17 Dexterity save or knocked prone.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Cantrip.** :: Casts a cantrip.
**Move.** :: Moves up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
**Thorn Lash (Costs 2).** :: Uses thorn whip.
**Healing Blessing (Costs 2).** :: Touches creature and heals 3d8+5 HP.
*"The forest remembers all debts—those paid and those owed."*
}}
{{pageNumber,auto}}

\page

### Physical Description
Towering and imposing (7'2", 280 lbs) with the gentle giant presence of firbolgs. Skin has gray-blue tone with texture resembling bark. Long hair and beard are dark brown with green moss growing naturally. Deep amber eyes that glow faintly in darkness. Face is weathered and lined with age, carved features like ancient wood. Wears robes of living vines that move slightly. The Thornwood Staff is gnarled oak that grows fresh thorns daily. Moves with slow, deliberate power. Smells of earth, moss, and ancient forests. Small plants occasionally sprout from his footprints.

### Equipment
- **Staff:** Thornwood Staff (legendary, carved from ancient oak, grows thorns, never breaks)
- **Armor:** Living Bark Armor (AC 16 with barkskin, regenerates daily)
- **Robes:** Druidic robes woven from living vines (deep green, always fresh)
- **Cloak:** Leaf Cloak (changes color with seasons, grants advantage on Stealth in forests)
- **Belt:** Rope of Entanglement (can animate as bonus action)
- **Pouch:** Component pouch with rare herbs, crystals, and seeds
- **Amulet:** Wooden Amulet (carved with druidic symbols, glows near unnatural magic)
- **Seeds:** Emergency goodberries (always has 10 fresh berries)
- **Book:** Personal journal of forest observations (50 years)
- **Tools:** Herbalism kit (expertly maintained)

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks in slow, measured tones
- Often pauses mid-sentence to listen to forest
- Refers to trees and animals by name
- Patient but can be terrifyingly angry when forest is threatened
- Quotes ancient druidic wisdom
- Makes decisions based on long-term forest health
- Treats all living things with respect

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Life and death, growth and decay—all part of the cycle."
- **Protection:** "The forest shelters us. We shelter the forest. This is the way."
- **Ancient Ways:** "The old ways preserved forests for millennia. Modern ways threaten them."
- **Debt:** "The forest remembers all debts—those paid and those owed."

**Bonds:**
- The entire forest (considers it a living entity)
- The druid circle (12 members under his guidance)
- Elder Thalindra Oakheart (ally in protecting nature)
- His sacred grove (contains 500-year-old trees)
- Ancient forest spirits (maintains communication with them)
- His apprentice druids (currently training 6 young druids)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes prioritizes forest over sentient life
- Holds grudges for decades (forest memory is long)
- Struggles to forgive those who harm nature
- Can be terrifyingly violent toward forest destroyers
- Inflexible about druidic traditions
- Doesn't trust civilization or technology

### Background & History
Thornwood isn't a name—it's what the forest itself calls him. He was born human, with a human name he's forgotten, in a village that no longer exists. When loggers came to clearcut his home forest, he called on power he didn't know he had. The forest responded. The loggers didn't survive.

That was sixty years ago. Since then, he's become more forest than man. Bark grows on his skin, leaves sprout from his hair, and he can be in any part of the forest simultaneously by traveling through the root network. He protects the woodland from all threats—natural and unnatural.

He's not hostile to civilization, but he's not friendly either. Loggers who harvest sustainably can pass safely; those who clear-cut wake the trees' wrath. Hunters who take only what they need are welcome; poachers are never found. He maintains balance, nothing more.

### Connections
- **Domain:** The entire old-growth forest (100 square miles)
- **Ally:** Forester Galen Sustainharvest (respects sustainable practices)
- **Circle:** Connection to other nature spirits
- **Enemy:** Quickcut Lumber Company (eternal vendetta)
- **Memory:** His human life (fading)

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Fading Humanity:** Will be entirely tree within twenty years. Unsure how to feel about it.
2. **The Logger Massacre:** What happened sixty years ago was worse than rumors suggest. Thirty-seven died.
3. **The Forest Heart:** Protects a grove that contains the forest's spiritual center. Would die for it.
4. **The Blight Knowledge:** Knows what's causing the blight but not how to stop it.
5. **The Successor Need:** Needs to pass his role to someone before he loses the ability. Looking for candidates.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Blight Cure:** Has partial information about stopping the blight. Needs help with the rest.
2. **The Forest Heart Defense:** Something is moving toward the grove. Needs powerful allies.
3. **The Successor Test:** Tests party members as potential successors to his role.
4. **The Quickcut War:** The lumber company is escalating. Needs help ending them permanently.
5. **The Humanity Question:** Reaches out about possibly regaining his human form. Conflicted about it.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Staff plants in ground during conversations (roots sprout)
- Small animals frequently around him
- Speaks to trees when alone (and they respond)
- Makes decisions agonizingly slowly
- Touches earth to sense disturbances
- Offers healing to injured animals reflexively
- Eyes glow green when angry

**Key Details:**
- Leader of western forest druid circle
- 127 years old, considered young for firbolgs
- Maintains sacred groves across 100-mile territory
- Can sense forest disturbances through root network
- Personal ally of Elder Thalindra
- Trained 30+ druids across his lifetime
- Has zero tolerance for illegal logging
- Forest spirits report to him

**Saving Throws** :: Dexterity +6, Wisdom +5, Charisma +8
**Skills** :: Acrobatics +6, Deception +8, History +9 (expertise), Insight +5, Perception +8 (expertise), Performance +11 (expertise), Persuasion +11 (expertise), Musical Instruments +9 (expertise)

***Memory Keeper.*** :: Can perfectly recall any story, song, poem, or historical account he's heard. His mind is a living library.
***Tongues Master.*** :: Can perform in any language he knows, translating on the fly.

***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two attacks with Rapier or casts a cantrip and makes one rapier attack.

***Special.*** :: This slender blade is covered in etched stories. On critical hit, target must succeed DC 16 Charisma save or be charmed for 1 minute.
***Vicious Mockery.*** :: Target within 60 ft. that can hear him must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or take 3d4 psychic damage and disadvantage on next attack roll.

***Enthralling Performance (1/Day).*** :: Performs for at least 1 minute. At end, up to 10 creatures who watched must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or be charmed for 1 hour. Charmed creatures regard him as friendly acquaintance.
***Tale of Heroes (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Tells inspiring battle story. All allies within 30 ft. gain:
- +2 to attack rolls
- +2 to AC
- Temp HP equal to 2d10+5
- Lasts 1 minute
### Reactions
***Countercharm.*** :: As reaction when ally within 30 ft. must make save against being frightened or charmed, can grant them advantage on save.
***Cutting Words.*** :: See special abilities above.
***Historical Insight.*** :: When ally within 30 ft. makes Intelligence check about history or lore, can use reaction to grant advantage.
*"Every tale deserves to be told, every song to be sung. Even the sad ones. Especially the sad ones."*
}}
{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

### Physical Description
Distinguished and charismatic (5'10", 160 lbs) with the ageless quality of half-elves. Silver-white hair worn long and theatrical. Sparkling blue eyes that dance with mischief and wisdom. Weathered face with laugh lines and a warm smile. Moves with performer's grace. Wears colorful traveling clothes that have seen a thousand performances. The legendary lute "Memoir" is always within reach. Hands show decades of instrument playing—callused but graceful. Smells of pipe smoke, old books, and campfire stories. Voice is rich, melodious, perfect for songs and tales.

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Fine Studded Leather (AC 13, decorated with story-telling scenes)
- **Weapon:** Storyteller's Rapier +1 (covered in etched tales, masterwork)
- **Secondary:** Hand Crossbow (for emergencies only)
- **Primary Instrument:** "Memoir" - Legendary Lute (masterwork, +2 to Performance, can cast legend lore 1/week)
- **Secondary Instruments:** Flute, hand drum, pan pipes (all masterwork)
- **Clothing:** Colorful traveling performer's outfit (worth 50 gp)
- **Hat:** Feathered cap (iconic, recognizable everywhere)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Many Colors (changes hue with mood)
- **Jewelry:** Multiple small trinkets (each with a story)
- **Books:** 12 leather journals (200+ years of chronicles)
- **Potions:** 2 potions of healing, 1 potion of inspiration (homebrew, grants inspiration die)
- **Other:** Sheet music, quills, ink, traveling performer's license

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks in dramatic, story-like fashion
- Makes callbacks to historical events he witnessed
- Breaks into song mid-conversation
- Collects stories like others collect coins
- Performs even mundane actions theatrically
- Remembers everyone's name and story
- Weeps openly at sad tales

**Ideals:**
- **Memory:** "Stories preserve what time erases. I am the keeper of memories."
- **Joy:** "In dark times, songs and stories are lights against the shadow."
- **Truth:** "Every story has truth in it, even the lies reveal character."
- **Connection:** "Through stories, we're all connected—past, present, future."

**Bonds:**
- His journals (200+ years of chronicles, irreplaceable)
- "Memoir" his legendary lute (gift from elven queen 150 years ago)
- The memory of loved ones long dead
- Every place he's performed (considers them home)
- Students he's taught the bardic arts
- The responsibility to preserve history

**Flaws:**
- Can't resist telling a story (even when inappropriate)
- Nostalgic to the point of melancholy
- Drinks too much when remembering sad tales
- Survivor's guilt (everyone he loved is dead)
- Lonely despite crowds (immortal among mortals)
- Secretly fears being forgotten
- Sometimes confuses memories across centuries

### Background & History
Finnegan has been collecting stories for forty years, traveling from village to village, tavern to tavern, gathering tales both true and legendary. He has one of the most comprehensive collections of folklore in Thaldros, and more importantly, he understands how to separate fact from fiction.

He was a soldier in his youth, then a failed merchant, before discovering his true calling: preserving oral tradition. He's not a great musician or performer—merely competent—but his knowledge of stories is encyclopedic. People invite him to perform because his tales are accurate and complete, even when the truth is uncomfortable.

Now sixty and slowing down, he's looking for a place to record his collection properly. He fears dying with his head full of stories that will be lost forever.

### Connections
- **Network:** Performers, storytellers, and archivists across the region
- **Patron:** Various nobles who fund his collection
- **Rival:** Other storytellers with less concern for accuracy
- **Friend:** Sage Elminster Runereader (scholarly collaboration)
- **Treasure:** Forty years of stories in his memory

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The True Histories:** Knows the real versions of many sanitized official histories. Dangerous knowledge.
2. **The Pattern Recognition:** Has noticed patterns in stories that suggest current events echo past catastrophes.
3. **The Hero's Secret:** Knows embarrassing truths about a famous hero's legend. Never told.
4. **The Dying Man's Confession:** Was told a deathbed confession that implicates a powerful family. Burden of proof.
5. **The Story Magic:** Some stories he tells have minor magical effects. Never examined why.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Recording Project:** Needs help establishing a proper archive before his memory fails.
2. **The Pattern Investigation:** Shares his pattern observations, hoping the party can investigate.
3. **The Dangerous Knowledge:** Has information about someone the party is investigating.
4. **The Confession Dilemma:** Wants advice on what to do with the deathbed confession.
5. **The Story Quest:** Heard of a legendary tale in a dangerous location. Needs escorts to collect it.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Strums lute while thinking
- Starts every statement with "I remember when..."
- Weeps during emotional stories (unashamed)
- Makes everything dramatic (even grocery shopping)
- Calls people "dear friend" after one meeting
- Breaks into relevant songs constantly
- Quotes his own compositions

**Speech Patterns:**
- "Ah, but that reminds me of a story from the Year of Falling Stars..."
- "As I sang to Queen Elara in '98, 'The past is never dead, it lives in song'..."
- "*strums lute* Let me tell you a tale..."
- "I was there, you know. I remember it well. *distant look*"

## Hermit Sage Morganna Whisperwind
*Medium humanoid (human), true neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 13 (16 with mage armor)
**Hit Points** :: 99 (18d8 + 18)
**Speed** :: 25 ft. (slowed by age)
![Hermit Sage Morganna Whisperwind](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-morganna-whisperwind.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 8 (-1) | 12 (+1) | 13 (+1) | 22 (+6) | 18 (+4) | 14 (+2) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +11, Wisdom +9
**Skills** :: Arcana +16 (expertise), History +16 (expertise), Insight +9, Investigation +11, Medicine +9, Nature +11, Perception +9, Religion +11
**Damage Resistances** :: Psychic
**Condition Immunities** :: None (deliberately refuses protections)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft. (magical), Passive Perception 19, can see magic auras
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Draconic, Celestial, Infernal, Abyssal, Deep Speech, Primordial, Ancient Common (pre-Worldrend), Telepathy 60 ft.
**Challenge** :: 9 (5,000 XP)
___
***Spellcasting.*** :: 14th-level wizard (School of Divination). Spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks.
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Light, Mage Hand, Message, Minor Illusion, Prestidigitation
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Detect Thoughts, Locate Object, See Invisibility
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Clairvoyance, Dispel Magic, Tongues
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Arcane Eye, Locate Creature
***5th level (2 slots).*** :: Contact Other Plane, Legend Lore, Scrying
***6th level (1 slot).*** :: Find the Path, True Seeing
***7th level (1 slot).*** :: Etherealness, Sequester
***Portent (2/Day).*** :: When she or creature she can see makes attack roll, ability check, or saving throw, she can replace the roll with one of two d20s she rolls at dawn. Must decide before roll is made.
***Expert Divination.*** :: When casts divination spell of 2nd level or higher, regains expended spell slot of lower level.
***The Third Eye (1/Short Rest).*** :: Can grant herself one of following benefits for 1 hour:
***Magical Longevity.*** :: Extended life through careful spellcasting and fey pacts. Ages 1 year per 10 years.
***Scholar's Mind.*** :: Perfect memory for anything read or studied. Can recall exact text from thousands of books.
***Prophetic Dreams.*** :: Each long rest, DM rolls twice for random encounter/event. She can choose which occurs, or neither.
***Forbidden Knowledge.*** :: Knows dangerous secrets about pre-Worldrend world, ancient rituals, true names, and lost magic.
***Library Network.*** :: Has created scrying links to 20 major libraries. Can research in any of them remotely.
### Actions
***Quarterstaff.*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d6-1 bludgeoning damage (1d8-1 versatile).::
***Cast a Spell.*** :: Casts a prepared spell.
***Prophetic Warning (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Uses divination magic to predict enemy's next action. One creature within 60 ft. must reveal their intended action next turn. Morganna's allies gain advantage against that action.
***Borrowed Knowledge (3/Day).*** :: Taps into collective knowledge of all libraries she's linked to. For 1 hour, has proficiency in any one skill, tool, or language of her choice.
***Consult the Tome (1/Day).*** :: Opens her ancient grimoire and consults forgotten lore. Casts legend lore without expending spell slot. Takes 1 minute.
### Reactions
***Shield.*** :: Casts shield to increase AC by 5 until start of next turn (spell).
***Forewarned.*** :: After rolling initiative, can swap initiative with one willing creature she can see.
***Prophetic Save.*** :: When ally she can see within 30 ft. fails saving throw, can use reaction to force reroll.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Cantrip.** :: Casts a cantrip.
**Move.** :: Moves up to half speed.
**Consult Knowledge (Costs 2).** :: Makes Intelligence check with advantage to recall lore.
**Scrying Glimpse (Costs 2).** :: Uses scrying to observe a distant location for 1 minute (must have been there before).
*"I have read every book worth reading twice. Some truths are found only in silence."*
}}

### Physical Description
Ancient and frail appearance (5'5", 110 lbs) despite magical longevity. Impossibly old for a human—312 years through magic and fey bargains. Hair is pure white, long and wild, often escapes from loose bun. Pale, paper-thin skin with age spots and wrinkles mapping centuries of study. Eyes are milky white (blind) but "see" through magical sight. Moves slowly, leaning on quarterstaff. Wears dusty gray robes covered in pockets containing scrolls, herbs, and oddities. Thick spectacles for reading (purely aesthetic, she "sees" magically). Smells of old parchment, dried lavender, and ancient dust. Trembling hands from age but mind is sharp as ever.

### Equipment
- **Staff:** Ancient Quarterstaff (simple, but has been with her 200+ years)
- **Robes:** Sage's Robes (AC 11, dusty gray, countless pockets)
- **Ring:** Ring of Mind Shielding (protects from thought reading, holds her soul if killed)
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Glasses:** Spectacles of True Seeing (allows true seeing 1/day)
- **Headband:** Headband of Intellect (already included in stats)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (advantage on Stealth, Perception can't see her)
- **Belt:** Belt of Many Pouches (contains spell components)
- **Books:** Personal grimoire (1,000 pages, 200+ years of notes)
- **Scrolls:** 10 scrolls of various divination spells
- **Potions:** 2 potions of longevity, 3 potions of healing
- **Library Key:** Master key that opens her hermitage library (3,000+ books)
- **Sending Stones:** 5 sending stones linked to other scholars
- **Telescope:** Astrological telescope (for star divination)

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks in slow, whispery voice
- Frequently forgets she's speaking aloud vs. thinking
- Quotes obscure texts constantly
- Forgets to eat unless reminded
- Obsessively organizes knowledge
- Intolerant of intellectual laziness
- Values truth above all else (even painful truth)

**Ideals:**
- **Knowledge:** "All knowledge must be preserved, even dangerous knowledge."
- **Truth:** "Truth is truth, whether comfortable or devastating."
- **Memory:** "I am the keeper of what was, so others may learn what will be."
- **Neutrality:** "I observe and record, I do not judge or interfere."

**Bonds:**
- Her library (3,000+ books, some unique copies)
- The truth about the Worldrend (obsessed with discovering)
- Her apprentices (she's trained 8 scholars across centuries)
- Ancient texts she hasn't finished reading
- The fey who granted her extended life (complicated relationship)
- Memories of everyone she's known (all dead now)

**Flaws:**
- Socially inept after centuries alone
- Values knowledge over people's feelings
- Hoards dangerous information
- Refuses to share certain secrets (even if it would help)
- Fears death will erase her accumulated knowledge
- Lonely but won't admit it
- Sometimes wishes she had let herself die naturally

### Background & History
Morganna was once a prominent healer in Silverpine, respected for her skill with both medicine and magic. Then she started hearing whispers—voices from dying patients, from the recently dead, from things that had never been alive. The voices drove her from the city, into the wilderness, where their chatter was quieter.

She's lived in her remote cottage for thirty years, visited only by those who need what she uniquely provides: healing for curses, potions that normal apothecaries can't make, and counsel from someone who hears both sides of the living and dead.

She's not mad—the whispers are real. She communes with spirits, ghosts, and stranger things. This has made her invaluable for certain problems and terrifying for most people. She's content with solitude; the living are exhausting, and the dead are usually more polite.

### Connections
- **Client:** Captain Marcus Frontiersman (provides control ritual)
- **Contact:** The Frost Seer Eirlys (fellow unusual seer)
- **Spirit Friends:** Several ghosts who provide information
- **Enemy:** A powerful ghost she bound that wants revenge
- **Worry:** The whispers are getting louder

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Bound Ghost:** Bound a dangerous ghost years ago. It's been working to escape.
2. **The Death Knowledge:** Has learned things about what lies beyond death. It's changed her.
3. **The Living Reluctance:** Has developed abilities that could help cities. Refuses to return.
4. **The Ritual Collection:** Has developed rituals for communicating with various entities. Some are dangerous.
5. **The Coming Dead:** The whispers are telling her about a massive influx of spirits soon. Mass death approaches.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Ghost Consultation:** Can contact specific dead for information. Services available.
2. **The Bound Ghost Crisis:** The imprisoned ghost is breaking free. Needs help reinforcing the binding.
3. **The Mass Death Warning:** Shares her warning about coming death. Needs help investigating.
4. **The Ritual Teaching:** Might teach spirit communication to those who prove worthy.
5. **The Marcus Emergency:** Something's wrong with Captain Marcus's ritual. Needs urgent ingredients.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Touches books lovingly
- Forgets people's names but remembers obscure facts
- Falls asleep mid-conversation (advanced age)
- Speaks to herself constantly
- Quotes book titles and page numbers
- Makes tea obsessively (has 40+ varieties)
- Writes notes constantly in margins

**Speech Patterns:**
- "As stated in Volume XII of Arcturus's Compendium, page 247..."
- "*mutters* Where did I put that reference...oh, you're still here?"
- "I read about this 180 years ago. Let me think... *long pause*"
- "Interesting. *writes note* Continue speaking."

## Archmage Veridian Starweaver (Expanded)
*Medium humanoid (elf), lawful neutral*
___
**Armor Class** :: 15 (18 with mage armor)
**Hit Points** :: 165 (22d8 + 66)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Archmage Veridian Starweaver (Expanded)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-archmage-veridian-starweaver.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 10 (+0) | 16 (+3) | 16 (+3) | 22 (+6) | 18 (+4) | 18 (+4) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +12, Wisdom +10, Charisma +10
**Skills** :: Arcana +18, History +12, Insight +10, Investigation +12, Perception +10
**Damage Resistances** :: Damage from spells (Magic Resistance)
**Senses** :: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 20
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Draconic, Celestial, Infernal, Sylvan, Dwarvish, Deep Speech
**Challenge** :: 18 (20,000 XP)
___
***Fey Ancestry.*** :: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
***Trance.*** :: Meditates 4 hours instead of sleeping.
***Spellcasting.*** :: 18th-level wizard. Spell save DC 20, +12 to hit with spell attacks.
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Fire Bolt, Light, Mage Hand, Prestidigitation, Ray of Frost
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*, Shield
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Detect Thoughts, Mirror Image, Misty Step
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Counterspell, Dispel Magic, Fireball
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Arcane Eye, Banishment, Greater Invisibility
***5th level (3 slots).*** :: Cone of Cold, Scrying, Wall of Force
***6th level (2 slots).*** :: Disintegrate, Globe of Invulnerability, True Seeing
***7th level (2 slots).*** :: Teleport, Plane Shift, Forcecage
***8th level (1 slot).*** :: Mind Blank*, Maze
***9th level (1 slot).*** :: Time Stop, Wish (rarely used)
***Magic Resistance.*** :: Advantage on saving throws against spells and magical effects.
***Arcane Recovery (1/Day).*** :: During a short rest, recovers expended spell slots up to 9th level combined.
***Signature Spells.*** :: Can cast Counterspell and Dispel Magic without expending spell slots (each 1/short rest).
***Scrying Network.*** :: Maintains 12 crystal balls across both kingdoms, can use as bonus action to switch views.
***Starweaver Bloodline.*** :: Once per day, can cast any divination spell without expending a spell slot.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Casts a cantrip and uses his Starlight Staff, or casts two cantrips.
***Starlight Staff (Quarterstaff +3).*** :: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 1d6+3 bludgeoning damage (1d8+3 versatile) plus 2d10 force damage.::
***Special.*** :: Functions as Staff of Power. Can cast wizard spells through the staff as a bonus action.
***Fire Bolt.*** :: Ranged Spell Attack: +12 to hit, range 120 ft., one target. ***Hit.*** 4d10 fire damage.::
***Cast a Spell.*** :: Casts a spell from prepared list.
***Teleportation Circle (Special).*** :: Can teleport party to any permanent circle he knows (costs 5,000 gp in materials, usually charges 1,000 gp per person).
### Reactions
***Shield.*** :: Casts Shield to increase AC by 5 until start of next turn.
***Counterspell.*** :: Automatically counters spells of 5th level or lower, makes check for higher levels (+12 bonus).
***Absorb Spell (Staff of Power, 3/Day).*** :: When targeted by a spell, absorb it into staff and regain spell slot equal to spell's level.
### Legendary Actions
Can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below. Only one legendary action can be used at a time and only at end of another creature's turn. Regains spent legendary actions at start of turn.
**Cantrip.** :: Casts a cantrip.
**Detect Magic.** :: Uses detect magic sense (knows presence of magic within 30 ft.).
**Teleport (Costs 2).** :: Uses misty step without expending a spell slot.
**Cast Spell (Costs 3).** :: Casts a spell of 3rd level or lower from prepared list.
*"Magic is not power. It is responsibility. Those who forget this truth become tyrants or corpses."*
}}

### Physical Description
Tall and slender (6'1", 145 lbs) with the timeless grace of high elves. Silver-white hair worn long and loose, often floating slightly as if in an invisible breeze. Eyes shift color with his mood - blue when calm, violet when using divination, gold when angry. Pale, ageless features marked with faint runic tattoos along his temples (warding glyphs). Wears flowing robes of deep midnight blue with silver star patterns that actually twinkle. The Starlight Staff pulses with gentle light and is never far from his hand.

### Equipment
- **Robes:** Archmage's Robes (AC 15 + Dex, advantage on saves vs. spells)
- **Staff:** Starlight Staff (Staff of Power, legendary, +3 quarterstaff, 20 charges)
- **Ring:** Ring of Spell Storing (contains Shield, Counterspell, Dispel Magic)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Protection +1
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Headband:** Circlet of Intellect (already included in stats)
- **Spellbook:** "The Cosmic Codex" - contains all wizard spells up to 9th level
- **Communication Crystals:** 12 sending stones linked to allies
- **Scrying Orb:** Crystal ball with true seeing
- **Potions:** 3 potions of supreme healing, 1 potion of invulnerability
- **Teleportation Chalk:** For creating temporary circles (10 uses)

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks in measured, precise sentences
- Makes direct eye contact that seems to see through deception
- Often pauses mid-conversation to consult magical sensors
- Gestures create small sparkles of light
- Has a dry, understated sense of humor
- Never panics - has seen too much

**Ideals:**
- **Responsibility:** "Those with power must use it to protect the powerless."
- **Knowledge:** "Understanding magic prevents its misuse."
- **Balance:** "Neither kingdom should dominate - equilibrium preserves peace."

**Bonds:**
- King Aldric IV (advised him since he was a child)
- The Kingdom of Thaldros
- His students and apprentices
- The truth about the Worldrend (obsessed with preventing repetition)
- Tower library (contains irreplaceable texts)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes too cautious, overthinks decisions
- Struggles to trust others with important tasks
- Secret guilt over not predicting something in the past
- Workaholic - sleeps only 4 hours per night
- Underestimates threats outside magical realm

**Expanded Role in Campaigns:**
**Primary Function:** High-level quest giver, magical expertise, investigation coordinator

**Key Details (Expanded):**
- Personal advisor to King Aldric IV
- Suspects Unbound infiltration of royal court
- Trained half the wizards in both kingdoms
- Tower in Kaer Thandros serves as adventure hub
- Possesses extensive scrying network
- Can teleport party to mission locations
- Maintains magical communication crystals

**Campaign Quest Types:**
1. **Investigation:** "Strange magical signatures detected - investigate source"
2. **Retrieval:** "Ancient artifact must be secured before Unbound finds it"
3. **Protection:** "Scholar in danger - escort them safely to my tower"
4. **Research:** "I need rare components/texts - can you acquire them?"
5. **Counter-intelligence:** "Spy among court wizards - identify them"

**Rewards Offered:**
- Spell scrolls and magical items
- Access to his personal library
- Training in advanced magic
- Teleportation services
- Introductions to other powerful allies
- Information about party's personal quests

**Relationship Progression:**
- **Suspicious** (first quest): Tests party's loyalty and competence
- **Interested** (after 2-3 quests): Offers better rewards, more trust
- **Allied** (after 5+ quests): Shares critical information, major support
- **Confidant** (late campaign): Reveals full knowledge of Unbound, recruits party for final missions

**Secrets He Can Reveal:**
- Lord Shadows Blackwood's true identity and motivations
- Location of pre-Worldrend artifacts
- Weaknesses of Unbound leadership
- Truth about Worldrend's cause
- Prophecies about Second Worldrend

**Connections:**
- Corresponds with Hermit Sage Morganna
- Knows The Frost Seer's visions are accurate
- Has met Matriarch Seraphina Silverleaf
- Studied under High Mage Arcturus (ghost) through séances
- Aware of Professor Miranda's research

---

### Background & History
Born over four centuries ago in the ancient elven city of Aethermere, Veridian showed prodigious magical talent before he could walk. He was formally inducted into the Arcanum at age forty (young for an elf), became a full wizard at one hundred, and achieved the rank of Archmage at two hundred and fifty—the youngest in recorded history.

His specialty is divination, but his true mastery lies in the intersection of magical schools. He developed the Starweaver Synthesis—a technique for combining spells of different schools into hybrid effects. The technique is now taught at every major magical academy, though few can replicate his fluency.

He has served as headmaster of the Silverpine Arcanum for seventy-five years, overseeing its expansion from regional school to continental institution. Under his leadership, enrollment has tripled, and the school has produced three archmages and dozens of notable wizards.

Despite his power, Veridian is approachable and patient with students. He remembers what it was like to struggle with concepts, even if it was four hundred years ago. His office door is always open, and he teaches at least one introductory class per term "to remember where magic begins."

### Connections
- **Sage Thelmar Runescribe:** His most promising former student, now serving the crown
- **Professor Elara Moonwhisper:** Faculty colleague who shares his interest in celestial phenomena
- **Archmage Eldrin Aethermere:** Secret correspondent in Aethoria, sharing research across the Sundering Sea
- **The Circle of Eight:** Rumored member, though he neither confirms nor denies
- **High Diviner Celestia Starborn:** His successor as head of Divination, though they disagree on methodology

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **Circle Membership:** He is indeed one of the Circle of Eight, though the organization operates more loosely than legends suggest.
2. **The Prophecy:** Has foreseen something catastrophic approaching within the next decade, but the vision is unclear and he fears acting on incomplete information.
3. **Aetherian Contact:** His correspondence with Archmage Eldrin involves more than research—they're developing a way to safely cross the Sundering Sea.
4. **Mortality's Approach:** Despite elven longevity, he can feel his time ending within the century. He's quietly preparing for succession.
5. **The Forbidden Research:** Keeps a sealed section in the library containing knowledge too dangerous to destroy but too dangerous to share.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Prophecy:** Veridian needs help investigating his unclear vision. The party might be pieces of the puzzle.
2. **The Crossing:** The Aetherian passage project is reaching a critical phase. He needs brave souls to test it.
3. **Succession Planning:** Time to identify and test the next headmaster. The candidates are all flawed in different ways.
4. **The Sealed Section:** Something has been disturbed in the forbidden library. Investigation required.
5. **Circle Business:** The other Circle members need a favor, and Veridian is calling in markers.

## Professor Miranda Questseeker (Expanded)
*Medium humanoid (human), lawful good*
___
**Armor Class** :: 13 (16 with mage armor)
**Hit Points** :: 78 (12d8 + 24)
**Speed** :: 30 ft.
![Professor Miranda Questseeker](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mixologee/tirvandor/main/tirvandor-project/core-rules/dungeon-masters-guide/images/npcs/tirvandor-npc-professor-miranda-questseeker.jpg){width:325px,mix-blend-mode:multiply}
___
|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 10 (+0) | 14 (+2) | 14 (+2) | 20 (+5) | 16 (+3) | 14 (+2) |
___
**Saving Throws** :: Intelligence +9, Wisdom +7
**Skills** :: Arcana +13, History +13, Investigation +13, Insight +7, Perception +7, Persuasion +6
**Senses** :: Passive Perception 17
**Languages** :: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Draconic, Ancient Common (pre-Worldrend dialect)
**Challenge** :: 9 (5,000 XP)
___
***Spellcasting.*** :: 9th-level wizard (Divination school). Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks.
***Cantrips (at will).*** :: Light, Mage Hand, Message, Prestidigitation
***1st level (4 slots).*** :: Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
***2nd level (3 slots).*** :: Detect Thoughts, Locate Object, See Invisibility
***3rd level (3 slots).*** :: Clairvoyance, Dispel Magic, Tongues
***4th level (3 slots).*** :: Arcane Eye, Locate Creature
***5th level (1 slot).*** :: Legend Lore, Scrying
***Expert Knowledge.*** :: Has advantage on all Intelligence checks related to history, arcana, and investigation. On a failed check, can reroll once per day.
***Researcher's Network.*** :: Can send messages to student assistants across both kingdoms. Within 24 hours, receives information as if casting Legend Lore (no spell slot needed, 1/day).
***Quick Study.*** :: Can learn one new language by studying for 1 week, or decipher unknown writing with 1 hour of study (DC 15 Intelligence check).
***Academic Authority.*** :: Has advantage on Persuasion checks when dealing with scholars, nobility, or in academic settings.
***Encyclopedic Memory.*** :: Can perfectly recall any text she's read. Has access to knowledge equivalent to a library in her mind.
### Actions
***Multiattack.*** :: Makes two dagger attacks or casts a cantrip and uses a dagger.
***Dagger +1.*** :: Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 20/60 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d4+3 piercing damage.::
***Light Crossbow.*** :: Ranged Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, range 80/320 ft. ***Hit.*** 1d8+2 piercing damage.::
***Cast a Spell.*** :: Casts a prepared spell.
***Share Knowledge (Recharge 5-6).*** :: Grants one ally advantage on their next Intelligence, Wisdom, or Charisma check as she provides relevant historical context or tactical advice.
### Reactions
***Defensive Scholar.*** :: When hit by an attack, can impose disadvantage on the attack roll (3/day). Represents ducking behind cover or using an object as a shield.
***Counterspell (3rd level).*** :: Can counter a spell of 3rd level or lower, or make a check (+9) for higher levels.
*"Every mystery has a solution. We simply must ask the right questions."*
}}

### Physical Description
Average height (5'6", 135 lbs) with an energetic, purposeful demeanor. Brown hair usually tied back in a practical bun, often with a quill stuck through it. Sharp hazel eyes behind round spectacles that seem to analyze everything. Wears practical scholar's robes in university colors (deep green and gold) with many pockets for note-taking supplies. Always has ink stains on her fingers. Carries a worn leather satchel full of books and papers. Moves with nervous energy, often gesturing enthusiastically when explaining discoveries.

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Bracers of Defense (AC 13 + Dex)
- **Weapons:** Dagger +1 (silver-inlaid, inscribed with runes), light crossbow
- **Ring:** Ring of Mind Shielding (thoughts can't be read, immune to detect thoughts)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (advantage on Stealth checks)
- **Spectacles:** Glasses of Seeing (advantage on Investigation and Perception checks involving sight)
- **Bag:** Bag of Holding (contains research materials, books, maps, artifacts)
- **Spellbook:** "The Investigator's Compendium" - Contains all her prepared spells plus 20+ utility spells
- **Research Materials:** Notebooks (12), quills, ink, chalk, measuring tools
- **Artifacts:** 3 minor pre-Worldrend artifacts she's studying
- **Potions:** 2 potions of healing, 1 potion of invisibility
- **Communication:** Sending stone linked to Archmage Veridian

### Personality
Traits
- Speaks rapidly when excited about research
- Constantly takes notes (even mid-conversation)
- Asks dozens of follow-up questions
- Gets distracted by interesting tangents
- Extremely organized despite appearing scattered
- Enthusiastic about mysteries

**Ideals:**
- **Truth:** "Knowledge must be preserved and shared, not hidden or destroyed."
- **Discovery:** "Every question answered reveals ten more questions. That's the joy of research."
- **Preservation:** "History forgotten is doomed to repeat."

**Bonds:**
- Silverpine University and its archives
- Her students (protective of them)
- The truth about House Blackwood
- Historical accuracy and record-keeping
- Hermit Sage Morganna (mentor figure)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes ignores danger when focused on research
- Naive about political dangers
- Trusts written sources too readily
- Workaholic who forgets to eat or sleep
- Uncomfortable in combat situations

### Background & History
Miranda earned her nickname honestly—she's never met a mystery she didn't want to solve or a question she wasn't willing to pursue across continents. Born in Crossvale to a merchant family, she rejected the family business at sixteen to attend the Arcanum, specializing in historical research and artifact identification.

Her breakthrough came at thirty-five when she correctly identified a "worthless" brooch in a museum collection as a pre-Worldrend communication device. The discovery made her reputation and funded her next twenty years of research.

Now fifty-eight, she holds the Chair of Ancient Studies at the Arcanum and has authored twelve books on pre-Worldrend civilizations. Her field expeditions are legendary—equal parts brilliant archaeological work and barely-survived disasters. Students compete fiercely for spots on her research teams.

Her methodology is controversial in academic circles. She believes in getting her hands dirty, taking calculated risks, and following hunches. "You can't understand history from a library chair," she's fond of saying. "You have to dig it up."

### Connections
- **Merchant Princess Yasmin:** Rival and occasional collaborator in artifact acquisition
- **Archmage Veridian Starweaver:** Mentor who indulges her unconventional methods
- **Caravan Master Hassan:** Has provided transport for several expeditions
- **Tomb Raiders Guild:** Complicated relationship—she buys from them while publicly condemning them
- **Research Assistants:** A rotating cast of graduate students who emerge from her expeditions either traumatized or transformed

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Part IV: NPCs}}
\page

{{descriptive
#### Secrets (DM Only)
1. **The Forbidden Dig:** Found a pre-Worldrend site five years ago that she's kept secret because what's there is too dangerous to excavate.
2. **The Tomb Raiders:** More than just a buyer—she founded the guild thirty years ago to fund her research, then "left" while keeping a controlling interest.
3. **Personal Tragedy:** Lost her husband and daughter on an expedition fifteen years ago. Threw herself into work to avoid dealing with grief she's never processed.
4. **The Artifact Collection:** Has a private collection of artifacts too dangerous or valuable to document publicly.
5. **Worldrend Knowledge:** Believes she knows what caused the Worldrend, but the implications are so disturbing she's never published her findings.
}}

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Forbidden Site:** She's finally ready to excavate, but needs a capable team to handle what's down there.
2. **The Guild Problem:** Someone is using her Tomb Raiders for something she didn't authorize. Time to investigate.
3. **Family Ghosts:** Evidence suggests her family might have survived the expedition. Or something wearing their faces has.
4. **The Publication:** She's decided to publish her Worldrend theory. Multiple parties want to stop her.
5. **Rival's Revenge:** Yasmin has discovered something Miranda wants desperately and is making her work for it.

### Roleplaying Notes
- Constantly adjusts her spectacles
- Mutters to herself when thinking
- Pulls out notebooks to reference previous findings
- Gets excited and talks faster
- Apologizes for going off on tangents
- Makes connections others miss

**Expanded Role in Campaigns:**
**Primary Function:** Investigation coordinator, research quest-giver, mystery solver

**Key Details (Expanded):**
- Leading expert on pre-Worldrend history
- Secretly investigating House Blackwood's fall
- Knows more about Unbound than she should
- Employs network of student researchers
- Has contacts in both kingdoms
- Often in danger due to discoveries
- Enthusiastic about hiring adventurers for field work

**Campaign Quest Types:**
1. **Archaeological:** "Ruins discovered - need exploration team"
2. **Historical:** "Interview survivors of [event] - record testimonies"
3. **Retrieval:** "Specific text/artifact needed for research"
4. **Protection:** "My research threatened - need guards"
5. **Investigation:** "Follow these leads - report findings"

**Research Topics (Quest Hooks):**
- House Blackwood's true fate and heir survival
- Pre-Worldrend civilization and technology
- Magical anomalies across both continents
- Dragon treaties and their violations
- Unbound faction activities (dangerous)
- Ancient prophecies about reunification

**Rewards Offered:**
- Historical knowledge and context
- Academic credentials (advantage on social interactions)
- Access to university restricted archives
- Letters of recommendation to nobility
- Payment in gold (university funded)
- Credit in published papers (fame)

**Character Development:**
- Starts as detached academic
- Becomes personally invested in stopping Unbound
- Eventually joins party as support NPC if convinced
- Can provide crucial breakthrough at key moment
- May be targeted for assassination (rescue mission)

**Secrets She Knows:**
1. Lord Shadows is legitimate Blackwood heir
2. Unbound seeking specific pre-Worldrend artifact
3. Location of House Blackwood's hidden vault
4. Truth about royal succession dispute
5. Pattern in magical disturbances (Second Worldrend signs)

**Connections:**
- Former colleague of Hermit Sage Morganna
- Corresponds with Archmage Veridian
- Knows Sage Elminster's research
- Has interviewed Captain Marcus about werewolves
- Student of historical figures through texts
